Organizational Law of the People's Political Council

Articles are Under Review

(Nanjing) The organizational law of the National People's Political Council has been approved in principle by the Central Political Committee, and 12 members including Ju Zheng and Chen Shuren have been appointed to review the articles. On the afternoon of the 24th, a meeting was convened by Committee Member Ju at the Central Party Headquarters to review the articles. It is said that the results showed that there were no major revisions to the original articles. According to Chen Shuren, the nature of the law is very similar to that of the National Assembly during the old government era in Beiping. Overseas Chinese compatriots occupied an important position in the revolutionary process of our party, and in principle should have the opportunity to participate in politics. This time, the organizational law of the People's Political Council stipulates that overseas Chinese will jointly elect eight representatives, which is very appropriate. The method of selecting overseas representatives will be determined by a separate election law, which is based on occupational groups and regional distribution. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

Provinces to Establish County Administration Construction Experimental Zones

Ministries of Interior, Finance, Implementation, and Education Agree on Four General Principles

(Nanjing) The methods for establishing county administration construction experimental zones in various provinces were discussed at a meeting convened by the Ministry of Interior on the 24th. Representatives from the Ministries of Interior, Finance, Implementation, Education, and the National Health Administration attended the meeting. Four general principles were decided upon, and a second meeting will be held on the 27th. The content of the general principles is as follows: 1. Each province may establish county administration construction experimental zones to improve the lives of local people and realize local construction. 2. The scope of the experimental zone is, in principle, based on the county as a unit, but may be expanded to several counties when necessary. After an experiment in one county proves effective, it should be extended to other counties at any time. 3. In order to compare the effects of the experiments and facilitate observation, each province may establish two or more experimental zones in areas with different customs and habits. 4. The selection of experimental zones should meet three or more of the following conditions to be considered qualified: (1) The situation in the area can represent the general situation of the province; (2) The area has previously handled local autonomy with relatively good results; (3) Local people understand autonomy and are able to contribute to it; (4) The autonomous experimental site has considerable equipment. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

Bazhong Has Been Recovered

Tian Songyao's Troops Enter the City

(Hankou) Liu Cunhou, representing Dong Yawei, received a telegram from Liu on the morning of the 24th, saying that Bazhong had been recovered, and Tian's troops had entered the city. Many people were killed, and corpses were lying across the streets. Refugees from the bandit areas are fleeing one after another. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

(Nanchang) Tian Songyao's representative, Wang Yate, met with Chiang to discuss the joint suppression of Xu, He, and Kuang bandits by Sichuan, Shaanxi, Hunan, and Hubei. The military discussion was very satisfactory. Wang immediately returned to Sichuan to report. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

Jinpu Railway

New Locomotives to Be Used

(Nanjing) The existing locomotives on the Jinpu Railway are insufficient. A portion was borrowed under the British Boxer Indemnity funds last spring. Eight "Mikado" type locomotives were ordered from the UK by the British Purchasing Committee. They have been shipped to Qingdao. The Machinery Department has ordered 160 technical workers from the Pukou, Jinan, and Tianjin three factories to rush to Qingdao to unload them together. After they are ashore, they will be transferred from the Jiaoji Railway to the Jinpu Railway and driven to Pukou for installation. However, because the newly purchased parts are not yet smooth, they must undergo several test runs before they can be officially used. In addition, 20 "Blue Steel" cars purchased earlier have been transported and are now in use. Eight heavy locomotives were also purchased from the UK last year for freight use, which are expected to arrive around June or July. After the new locomotives are in operation on April 1st, the train speed can be increased. The current direct train between Beiping and Pukou takes 36 hours, but will only take 27 hours in the future. More than 500,000 railway ties along the route have also been replaced, and the Yangtze River ferry has transported and installed them. Direct train service between Shanghai and Beiping will be available in July, and the travel time will be at least 40 hours. In addition, along the Jinpu Railway, there are often poor people who cannot afford tickets and climb onto the roofs and bottoms of the cars at each station when the train is about to depart, which is extremely dangerous. It is now planned to allocate old cars to run "poor people's cars" in sections after the new locomotives are replaced. The railway is also uniting with various sectors in Pukou to organize a relief association to rescue petty thieves and those who come to the association for help. 1. Those who are unable to return home will be sent back to their hometowns by the association. 2. Those who are homeless and of strong build will be sent to the municipal government to work as road construction workers. 3. Those who are disabled and homeless will be sent to relief homes. 4. Those who are willing to learn crafts will be sent to training institutions. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

Incidental Civil Suits

Must Be Accepted and Adjudicated by the Criminal Court

Unless it is determined to be truly complicated, it may not be transferred to the civil court for trial. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Xu Shaozhen is 73 years old and still in good spirits, but his leg ailment has not healed. At the end of the Qing Dynasty, Xu served as the Commander of the 9th Division. During the Xinhai Revolution, he led troops to attack Yuhuatai in Nanjing. After the establishment of the Republic of China, he served as the Commander-in-Chief of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Allied Forces and the Garrison Governor. When Yuan Shikai betrayed the country by establishing the Hongxian monarchy, he strongly invited Xu to serve as the Chief of the General Staff. Xu denounced his delusions and did not accept the offer. In the sixth year of the Republic, Xu served as the Commander-in-Chief of the Guangdong Garrison, the Governor of Guangdong Province, and the Minister of Interior. In the twelfth year of the Republic, he went north to see the Prime Minister when he was ill. After the Prime Minister passed away, he retired to Shanghai to live a simple life. At 2:00 p.m. on the 24th, Sun Ke personally visited him. The National Government will hold Xu's inauguration ceremony next Monday. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

Draft Registration Measures for Sailing Vessels

(Nanjing) According to a report from the Inspector General of Customs to the Ministry of Finance, in order to prevent tax evasion by sailing vessels transporting goods, draft registration measures have been formulated. All sailing vessels with a carrying capacity of two dans or more must be registered with the Customs. Otherwise, if they are caught, they will be treated as smuggling. The Ministry has issued a circular to all Customs offices to implement this measure uniformly. (February 24th Special Dispatch)

During Mr. Yan's absence from Moscow, the affairs of the Chinese Embassy will be handled by Counselor Wu Nanru. (February 24th Reuters) Roosevelt Decides on Policy Guidelines

Solving World Economic Problems

As the Main Focus for the Next Four Years

New York, February 23rd. Friends of US President-elect Roosevelt predicted today that after the Democratic Party government takes office on March 4th, the first things to be implemented will be (1) major changes in overseas representatives, (2) close cooperation between the State Department and the Treasury Department, effectively forming a supreme diplomatic agency, (3) abolishing the long-standing most-favored-nation clause policy. They believe that Roosevelt originally intended to appoint Hull as Treasury Secretary, but in view of the fact that most diplomatic issues in the next four years will be related to the economy, he was appointed as Secretary of State. Hull also wants Dr. Morey of Columbia University to be the Assistant Secretary of State. Furthermore, the appointment of Wording as Treasury Secretary can also be seen as proof that the Treasury Department will cooperate with the State Department to solve diplomatic problems, because Wording was previously rumored to be appointed as the Ambassador to the United Kingdom. As for the current diplomatic issues, in addition to the undeclared wars in South America and the Far East, the rest are all economic in nature. It is said that Roosevelt will immediately begin to handle these issues in the most direct and informal way after taking office, and all diplomatic policies will be decided by the President in consultation with the State Department and the Treasury Department. It is expected that the issues to be addressed within two months of Roosevelt's inauguration include (1) striving to negotiate a general reduction of tariffs by various countries (a separate tariff agreement for sugar will be drawn up), (2) recognizing Soviet Russia, (3) resolving war debts, (4) negotiating special measures with various countries to revitalize US foreign trade (these measures will likely replace the commonly used most-favored-nation clause with reciprocal agreements), (5) persuading major countries that have abandoned the gold standard to return to the gold standard, (6) seeking a truce in South America and determining a Far East policy, (7) finally deciding on the issue of joining the International Court of Justice. As for overseas representatives, Mellon's appointment as Ambassador to the United Kingdom is entirely due to political relations and will leave office with the Republican government. His successor is rumored to be Judge Pinghan, the publisher of the Louis Fiel Post. Davis will still serve as the representative to important European meetings, and Davis has already agreed.

(Reuters, New York) Professor Raymond Moley of Columbia University will be one of the most powerful figures in the new government in the future. Although it cannot be determined at present what kind of position he will hold, it is believed that after Roosevelt takes office on the 4th of next month, he will still be one of Roosevelt's plenipotentiary advisors. After Roosevelt's election victory, Moley has been planning for him almost every day until now. When Roosevelt discussed war debts at the White House last November, Moley was his only assistant. Three months ago, almost no one in the United States knew Moley's name, but today Moley is famous throughout the country. During the campaign, he drafted more speeches for Roosevelt than anyone else. He is a versatile writer and a master of words, and he is good at drafting moving texts, so he has been of great help to Roosevelt's position. After the election ended, Roosevelt and Dr. Moley became even closer. Now Roosevelt consults Moley on almost everything, and Moley's proposals are becoming more and more influential. Obviously, in the next few years, we will often come into contact with Moley's actions and words. He is of medium height and weight, his face is dark but very clean, his eyes are bright, and he has an approachable attitude. Although he has received a high level of education, he is not arrogant. He is 46 years old and began teaching political science as an assistant professor at Columbia University in 1923. He is now a professor of public law. He has written many books and commented on government and politics. He also studies criminology. In his autobiography, he refused to reveal his beliefs in religion and politics. Roosevelt intends to invite him to join the new government so that he can exchange ideas with him during his entire term. Moley has agreed to this.

World's Large-Scale

Drug Manufacturing Plant

Difficult to Develop in Central Europe and the Near East

Headquarters to Be Established in Shanghai and Tianjin Concessions

Kaifeng, February 23rd, National News Agency. Russell Pasha, the Chief of Police of Cairo, Egypt, is one of the most effective fighters against drugs in the world. He has cracked down on international drug trafficking organizations. It is reported that Pasha will soon submit a report to the League of Nations on the situation of the world's drug trade. Although the contents of the report are not known in detail, it is said that Pasha has described the history of the world's large-scale drug manufacturing plants, saying that they were first established in Switzerland, but after being discovered by the Swiss authorities, they were banned. The plant then moved to Turkey, where three large factories were established. Later, Pasha reported this to Turkish President Kemal, and they were also closed down. Not long ago, the plant had moved to Bulgaria, but as a result of Pasha's continued efforts, its business situation was far less favorable than before. Recently, because it is difficult to develop in Europe, it plans to move to the Far East and establish a headquarters. It is said that it is seriously considering operating in the concessions of Shanghai or Tianjin, because concessions seem safer, and at least in the near future, they are unlikely to be interfered with by the police.

Disarmament Conference

French Proposal Passed

Only Germany Voted Against

Geneva, February 23rd, Reuters. The French proposal to establish standards for the armies of European and other continental countries, shorten the term of military service, and reduce the number of standing troops was passed today by the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference. Only Germany voted against it. Before the vote, the dispute between France and Germany over the order of discussing troop strength and weapons was raised again. But after a long discussion, British Under-Secretary of State Eden said, "If we continue to argue like this, the final solution will only be left to our descendants."

Headquarters of the German Communist Party Sealed

Berlin, February 24th, Reuters. The headquarters of the German Communist Party was sealed today by the authorities, pending further orders. The reason is that the headquarters had issued seditious leaflets.

Japan Plans to Strengthen Mechanized Corps

Large-Scale Cavalry Maneuvers to Begin in Mid-October

Aiming to Invade North China and Siberia

Tokyo Correspondence. Since the Japanese Ministry of the Army announced its military reform plan, it has stepped up its preparations for war against China and the Soviet Union. It believes that the main weapons for invading North China and attacking Siberia are tanks and armored vehicles. Since the September 18th Incident, Japan has indeed ordered a general mobilization to increase the production of mechanized weapons, rushing to manufacture them day and night. For example, the Ishikawa Island Shipyard has now completed part of the order, including 350 new tanks and more than 500 armored vehicles. The weapons are transported by military train to the Asahikawa area of Hokkaido to begin cold-weather exercises. The exercises began on January 10th, using the heavy snowstorm on January 26th as a special tactical exercise. Participants included tanks, tractors, armored vehicles, military trucks, ordinary cars, and motor vehicles from the Setagaya Motor Vehicle School. From the 28th, the entire First Division, the Setagaya Motor Vehicle School, the Matsudo Engineering School, the Narashino Cavalry School, the Chiba Infantry School, and the Tokorozawa and Shimoshi Flying Schools were mobilized in the Tokyo area for a large-scale scientific mechanized corps exercise in the Omiya and Chiba areas. Also on January 28th, a street battle exercise with tanks was held in Yokosuka. In addition, in order to facilitate the invasion of Siberia and North China, the cavalry force is actively strengthened. It is planned to mobilize the 1st, 15th, 16th, 8th, 22nd, 24th, and 2nd cavalry regiments to hold a special cavalry exercise in mid-October this autumn. (Chinese Allied Press)

Great Alliance of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou

Cooperation Regulations Formulated by Liu Xiang

Joint Office of the Three Provinces to Be Established

Chongqing Airmail. The Sichuan War has ended early, and is gradually restoring to its pre-war state. The war in Guizhou Province has also come to an end due to the support of the Guangxi faction for Wang Jialie. Only the remnants of Che Mingyi's troops on the western route have not been completely eliminated. The Yunnan Province has been relatively calm since Long Yun took office. However, Long recently felt isolated and unable to cope with the environment, so he advocated a great alliance of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces in order to maintain the current situation and prevent changes. It is said that Wang Jialie expressed great agreement with Long's proposal, and Liu Xiang also agreed to Sichuan's participation. Therefore, Long Yun sent representative Lu Shouchi, Wang Jialie sent representative Xu Daowei, and Liu Xiang sent representative Lin Bixian to exchange views and reach a consensus, and jointly formulated the Temporary Regulations on Cooperation between Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou Provinces for compliance. The contents are as follows: (Article 1) These regulations are jointly formulated by Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces, and are named the Joint Regulations of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou Provinces. (Article 2) The purpose of these regulations is to promote cooperation and joint liaison between Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces, stabilize the local area, promote military and civilian administration, consolidate the border, and relieve the central government's worries about the west. (Article 3) These regulations are jointly initiated and formulated by Liu Xiang of Sichuan, Long Yun of Yunnan, and Wang Jialie of Guizhou. After implementation, Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces shall abide by them consistently and shall not violate them. (Article 4) Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces shall take consistent action on all foreign matters. The representatives stationed in various places shall have consistent opinions and shall not be divided. (Article 5) Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces shall jointly unite and jointly run all production matters within the three provinces. (Article 6) Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces shall unite and jointly suppress bandits within the territory, regardless of jurisdiction. (Article 7) These regulations shall be briefly applicable before the official establishment of the joint office of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces. (Article 8) These regulations shall take effect after being signed, sealed, and promulgated by the authorities of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces. (Article 9) These regulations shall become invalid after the official cooperation regulations of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces are produced.

The above temporary regulations have been recognized and implemented by Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou provinces. Liu Xiang, Wang Jialie, and Long Yun are currently preparing to establish a joint office of the three provinces, and are preparing to hold a joint conference of Sichuan, Yunnan, and Guizhou in March. (February 23rd)

Local News 6

Aviation Association Regularly Begins Recruiting Members

Recruitment Methods Have Been Drafted

Inviting Team Leaders for a Group Meal

Since the China Aviation Association announced the list of team leaders for member recruitment, the detailed methods for recruitment have also been drafted. Wu Tiecheng, the chief team leader of the recruitment team, is scheduled to host the team leaders at the YMCA on Baixianqiao at 4 PM today, to start the process as soon as possible. The recruitment methods are as follows:

Ordinary membership dues: Two yuan per year. Special membership: Ten yuan per year. Supporting membership: Fifty yuan per year. Permanent membership: A one-time payment of five hundred yuan. Military and police membership: One yuan per year. Members will receive a commemorative badge from the China Aviation Association after joining (Major donors will receive special thanks).

The period is from March 1st to April 30th. Each team will report its fundraising results every ten days, which will be announced in the newspaper, and competitive incentives will be established to encourage participation.

The minimum target is two hundred teams. Mayor Wu is the chief team leader, and Wang Zhengting is the chief consultant. The list of team leaders has been announced. Additional teams are welcome, with the goal of making membership accessible to everyone.

Team leaders and members who collect funds will have membership application forms. During recruitment, they will ask applicants to sign and pay the fee, which the team leader will submit daily to designated banks for collection and issue receipts. The China Aviation Association will then register them separately and send commemorative badges and membership certificates to the members. These donations will be used entirely for purchasing aircraft.

The general office of the recruitment team is located at the YMCA on Baixianqiao, the publicity department is located at the Intelligence Agency (Dalu Commercial Market, No. 308), the finance department is located at the Municipal Government, and the fundraising department is located at the Bankers Association.

Yesterday, the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau

Hosted Newspaper Reporters

The Director Reported That the Expansion Budget Requires 480,000 Yuan. Our Country Is Not Without Manufacturing Talent, Only Lacking Funds.

The Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau, after the merger of the Fuzhou Shipping Bureau and Shanghai, was ordered to relocate in the spring of the 20th year of the Republic. Since then, it has strived to expand and actively develop, and has added a sales department to formulate various plans. Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, it invited newspaper reporters to visit the manufacturing bureau. The bureau provided a small steamboat to pick up and drop off at the Customs Wharf. More than forty reporters from various newspapers arrived at the naval dock and visited the facilities until 5 PM. The details are as follows:

Reporting the Progress After the newspaper reporters landed, they were received by the Director Zeng Yijing and the engineers of the entire factory. Director Zeng reported that the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau was founded in the spring of the 7th year of the Republic, originally located in Fuzhou, and manufactured various types of aircraft, including trainers and military aircraft, all of which were used by the Naval Aviation Department and praised by the aviation community at home and abroad as the only domestic aircraft manufacturing factory in China. In the spring of the 20th year, the Navy Department regarded Shanghai as an important commercial port in China, and the Shanghai Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau had a large base and convenient land and water transportation, and the workers of the Jiangnan Shipyard could assist, so it ordered the Fuzhou Aircraft Manufacturing Factory to move to Shanghai and merge, so as to facilitate expansion and active development. In recent years, enthusiastic people from all walks of life have advocated aviation to save the country and strive to increase strength, but the purchase of various types of aircraft is mostly from abroad, which inevitably leads to the outflow of rights and interests. The bureau has now set up a sales department to design drawings and manufacture various types of aircraft for all sectors of society, and has formulated an expansion plan. Our country is not without manufacturing talent, but we feel that we are hampered by (1) the problem of raw materials, such as steel and hardware, which are lacking in domestic production, and (2) the problem of funding, which is entirely dependent on the Navy Department's insufficient funding for development, which has prevented the immediate implementation of the plan. Now, we hope that all sectors of society will assist in advocating domestic aircraft manufacturing, so that even if it is still in its infancy, it will soon be comparable to foreign countries.

Expansion Plan Formulated by Director Zeng Yijing

The plan to expand the manufacturing of aircraft is as follows: to expand the factory so that it can produce 24 aircraft per year, including trainers, fighters, reconnaissance aircraft, bombers, etc. The budget (3) regarding the purchase of machinery, tools, and the most needed raw materials: (1) 150,000 yuan for wood; (2) 200,000 yuan for steel; (3) 50,000 yuan for various equipment, totaling 400,000 yuan. (B) Regarding the manufacturing workshop: (1) The area of the factory building is 11,600 square feet, costing 50,000 yuan to build; (2) The assembly plant is about six aircraft positions, with an area of 4,200 square feet, costing 25,000 yuan to build; (3) The material warehouse has an area of 1,500 square feet and costs 6,000 yuan to build, totaling 81,000 yuan. The total is 481,000 yuan.

The cost of each aircraft: The Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Bureau's estimated prices for manufacturing various types of aircraft are as follows: (1) 125-horsepower trainer, 24,000 yuan; (2) 210-horsepower advanced trainer, 28,000 yuan; (3) 500-horsepower fighter, 110,000 yuan; (4) 550-600 horsepower bomber, 130,000 yuan; (5) 500-horsepower reconnaissance aircraft, 120,000 yuan.

Leading the Tour Then, Director Zeng Yijing and engineer Ma Shude led the tour, explaining in detail the various aircraft samples on display and the various types of seaplanes and land planes parked at the aviation department, including the Jiang'ou bomber, the Jiangpeng trainer, the Jiangjing, the Jiangyang, the Jiangyan reconnaissance aircraft, the Jiangyi, the Jiangfeng, the Jianghong trainer and reconnaissance aircraft, the Jianghe, and other nine aircraft, as well as various manufacturing workshops, such as the woodworking factory and the assembly factory. Refreshments were served around 4 PM, and the tour concluded at 5 PM. The reporters then took a group photo with Director Zeng and dispersed.

The Remaining 60,000 Troops of Wang Delin's Army

Are Still Fighting Fiercely in Eastern Jilin

Song Yunzhang Came to Shanghai Seeking Aid

Wu Yicheng Telegraphed the Battle Situation

Wang Delin, commander-in-chief of the Jilin National Salvation Army, was forced to retreat from his defensive position in Suifenhe on the eighth of last month due to enemy pressure and lack of ammunition and supplies. They divided their forces and used collaborators as their wings, launching a four-pronged attack on our army's bases in Dongning and Suifen Town on January 1st. Yicheng supervised the front line and fought fiercely with the enemy for four days and nights. They pressed forward in succession, with heavy casualties on both sides. Two enemy planes were shot down by us, and more than half of the enemy cavalry was wiped out by our army. At a moment of life and death, the rear of Dongning reported repeated emergencies, and we had to divide our forces to provide reinforcements. Unexpectedly, Dongning fell to the enemy on January 8th after three days and nights of resistance. On the afternoon of the 9th, our solid positions in Suifen Town and Tianqiao Town were breached by the enemy, and the flanks were threatened. Countless officers and soldiers were killed in action, and after running out of ammunition and supplies, they had no choice but to retreat in different directions. They were then blocked by enemy troops. Our Commander-in-Chief Wang, Deputy Commander Kong, and the various brigades and regiments of our army were cut off from contact. Yicheng rushed to Ning'an through a side road, reorganized more than 30,000 troops, and ordered the eastern route to concentrate on the north bank of the Mudan River, and the western route to concentrate on Dunhua and Emu County. More than 10,000 people remained stationed in the Anhua area and came to ask for orders. Yicheng was planning to advance and cooperate with the friendly forces in southwestern Liaoning and southern Manchuria when he received Commander-in-Chief Wang's order to go to the inland and various mass organizations to report on the army's operations over the past year and to discuss relief plans. All responsibilities of the Commander-in-Chief of the Chinese National Salvation Army were delegated to the commander-in-chief of the front line. The various brigades and regiments of Suining Wangyan were to be controlled and dispatched. Therefore, Yicheng not only had the task of advancing westward, but also the planning of the eastern front. How could a man of mediocre talent shoulder such a huge responsibility? However, since the September 18th Incident, there have been no less than 250,000 anti-Japanese self-defense troops in the three northeastern provinces, but they have been destroyed by the enemy one after another. Now, the only relatively complete and powerful forces are the volunteers in southern Manchuria.

Ningbo Fellow-Townsmen Association

Establishes Aviation to Save the Country Fundraising Committee

Plans to Divide Into 500 Destroyer Squads

And 200 Fighter Squads

The Aviation to Save the Country Fundraising Committee, organized by the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Townsmen Association, is ready. Yesterday, a meeting was held to discuss the matter. The committee members present included Zhang Shenzhi, Wu Yaqin, Ye Xianggao, Mao Heyuan, Hu Yongjing, Zhu Meixian, Jin Runxiang, Ren Jinpin, Mu Zixiang, Sun Meitang, Chen Qibo, and more than 30 others. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Shenzhi, and the proceedings were carried out in accordance with the usual etiquette. (A) Matters reported: 1. The Aviation to Save the Country Fundraising Committee has been formally established on the second floor of the Fellow-Townsmen Association and has begun its work. 2. Chen Qibo was publicly elected as the director-general, and Lin Mianzai, Liu Zhixiang, Dong Xinqin, and Zhang Zeda were elected as directors. (B) Matters resolved: 1. To convene a general meeting of the entire association at 2 PM on March 5th to actively carry out the fundraising. 2. To conduct national salvation fundraising in a squadron system, so as to achieve the effect of gathering the strength of the masses. A total of 500 destroyer squadrons are planned, with each squadron raising more than 200 yuan (more than 100,000 yuan in total). 200 fighter squadrons are planned, with each squadron raising more than 500 yuan (more than 100,000 yuan in total), for a total of more than 200,000 yuan. (C) Committee Member Zhang Shenzhi proposed the association's charter, which was approved. The rest is omitted. The charter is recorded below: [Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Townsmen Association Aviation to Save the Country Fundraising Committee Charter] Article 1: This association is initiated by fellow-townsmen in Shanghai, with the purpose of raising funds to purchase aircraft, and is named the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Townsmen Association Aviation to Save the Country Fundraising Committee. Article 2: The purpose of this association is to strengthen air defense and jointly share the national crisis. Article 3: There is no fixed number of committee members in this association. All fellow-townsmen who are enthusiastic about saving the country may be appointed. Article 4: This association has one chairman, who is elected by the committee members. Article 5: This association is divided into the following sections: A. General Affairs Section; B. Registration Section; C. Custody Section; D. Publicity Section. Each section has one director and one deputy director, who are elected by the committee members. Article 6: This association has one director-general and several directors to handle daily affairs. Article 7: The fundraising goal of this association is 200,000 yuan, divided into two types of squadrons: fighter squadrons and destroyer squadrons. Fighter squadrons must raise at least 500 yuan, and destroyer squadrons must raise at least 200 yuan. Each squadron has one captain and several members. There is no fixed number of squadrons. Article 8: Squadrons with outstanding achievements will be rewarded separately. The reward methods will be formulated separately. Article 9: The association's office is located on the second floor of the Ningbo Shanghai Fellow-Townsmen Association on Xizang Road. Article 10: This charter will be implemented after being approved by the general meeting. If there are any omissions, they may be amended at any time.

The Northeast Association Issued a Declaration

Stating the Purpose of Establishment and the Responsibilities Undertaken

Hoping for Unity From Top to Bottom and National Mobilization

The Northeast Association issued a declaration yesterday, stating the purpose of its establishment and the responsibilities it undertakes. The full text is as follows:

The Northeast has been occupied for two years, and the bloodshed in Shanghai has lasted for more than a year. The result of our country's long-term struggle is only that the enemy's flames have become more intense and the national crisis has deepened. In recent months, the enemy has reoccupied Yu Pass, coveted eastern Hebei, attacked Rehe, and plotted for North China. An unprecedented war has already broken out. If we do not concentrate our national strength and resist to the death, not only will the Northeast have no hope of recovery, but North China will also suffer miserably. Once North China is lost, the future of the country will be unpredictable. This is why the whole country is unanimously advocating active resistance as the only way to save ourselves. However, in order to implement resistance and not stop until the goal of victory is achieved, there are three major prerequisites: (1) The whole country must be permanently united. The reason why the national crisis is so serious and the enemy slanders us as an unorganized country is that this righteousness has not been fully demonstrated. This is also what the people of the country have been consistently demanding in recent years. Fortunately, the whole country has recently awakened and is becoming increasingly unified. We hope that from now on, disputes will be eliminated forever and unity will be maintained from beginning to end. (2) The hearts of the people of the whole country must be permanently unwavering. Since the Opium War, our country has experienced national disasters such as the Sino-Japanese War and the Boxer Rebellion. We should all learn from the pain and work hard to overcome difficulties. However, the habit of being cowardly and seeking temporary ease has deeply rooted in the hearts of the people and cannot be reinvigorated, which has led foreigners to ridicule us as having "five minutes of hot blood." The previous events of boycotting goods are proof that their words are not without reason. If we do not wash away the long-standing habit of seeking temporary ease and persevere to the end in future struggles, the country will be destroyed in no time, let alone resist. (3) All parts of the country must be mobilized in unison. The scope of the current resistance war is expanding, and it is difficult to predict how long it will last. However, it can be asserted that it cannot be resolved in the short term. Therefore, the armies in all parts of our country must be mobilized in unison, and the people in all parts of the country must also be prepared in unison in order to implement long-term resistance and achieve final victory. All three of these depend on the mutual promotion of the compatriots of the whole country, and then we can expect them to succeed. We, the members of this association, are willing to work with the compatriots of the whole country to fulfill this unique duty. This is the first reason why this association was established. Even if the resistance struggle can be implemented, there are three things that our compatriots should pay special attention to in order to seek final victory, which is absolutely in our hands: (1) All the people of the country must contribute money if they have money, and strength if they have strength, to support the government. And the financial resources must be concentrated and used properly in order to achieve the greatest effect. Since the national crisis, the spirit of the people in the mainland and overseas Chinese to donate money to resist Japan is not lacking in courage, and the organizations that work hard to support them in various places and groups are also not lacking in number. However, they are either limited to a certain time or a certain event, and gradually decline after the time has passed, or they are limited to a certain place or a certain corner, and the people's strength needs to be further promoted. Now that the national crisis is becoming more urgent and the war is deepening, it is necessary to have a permanent and unified national system of the people to unite the national strength and create long-term anti-Japanese resources. (2) It is necessary to continue to support the armed comrades who have been resisting Japan in the Northeast from beginning to end. The volunteer army in the Northeast has been fighting hard for many years, and the strength lies in the joint efforts of the army and the people. Although the withdrawal of generals such as Ma Su, Feng, and Li from the Northeast has caused the anti-Japanese forces to suffer setbacks, the anti-Japanese spirit of the hundreds of thousands of armed people scattered in the three provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang is still extremely enthusiastic, and the latent power is growing. However, what they need is the active replenishment of ammunition, and what they are looking forward to is the government's dispatch of troops to suppress the rebellion. Now that they hear that the war has started on the border of Rehe, they will surely rejoice and be willing to take up arms to lash out at the tyranny and use their armor and sharp weapons to contain the enemy troops, which is most conducive to the military opportunity. Therefore, continuous support is of utmost importance. (3) It is necessary to gradually strengthen and popularize moral assistance internationally. According to recent news from Geneva, the League of Nations has made a judgment and determined what is right and wrong. Our country has received great international moral assistance. However, the international situation is changing rapidly, and the effort to survive depends on ourselves. As long as we can fight to the death and give the tyrannical Japan a major blow, which friendly country in the world will not help us? Otherwise, if we do not make up our minds and rely on others every day, friendly countries will also have the pain of being unable to help. In the future, we will only use the strength of the whole country to deal with the tyrannical Japan, and use self-help to seek the country, so that we can gradually strengthen and popularize moral assistance internationally. All three of these depend on the efforts of the people of the whole country, and then we can expect them to be realized. We, the members of this association, are even more willing to bear this greatest responsibility with the compatriots of the whole country. This is the second reason why this association was established. The national crisis has been going on for seventeen months now. The sacrifice of the lives and property of our people is almost incalculable, and the sacrifice to recover the lost territory in the future may be a thousand or a hundred times greater than this. With such a great sacrifice, how can we be willing to recognize that the Northeast has become a land of de facto international co-management? Moreover, the corner of the Northeast is not only related to the prosperity and decline of our entire country, but also has a major impact on the changes in the overall situation in East Asia and the world. If it is not fundamentally and reasonably resolved, the seeds of disaster are lurking, and it is bound to become the fuse of an international war and endanger world peace. Therefore, in addition to actively recovering the lost territory and defending the territory, we should also thoroughly study the future development of the Northeast and its relationship with the world. All of our people should take this as their own responsibility. This is the third reason why this association was established. In short, the national crisis will not end until the Japanese pirates are eliminated, and for the sake of national survival and national freedom, any sacrifice is worth it. Now that the hot war has broken out, in order to implement the struggle of active resistance and achieve final victory, we must unite from top to bottom, be permanently unwavering, mobilize all parts of the country in unison, and contribute money if we have money, and strength if we have strength, and seek the country through self-help. In the future, the solution to the Northeast problem and its future development will be a heavy responsibility and a long way to go for the people of the country. The situation is urgent and compelling, and there is no time to hesitate. Only our people can rise up and plan for it. Members of the Northeast Association: Shi Liangcai, Wang Xiaolai, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Zhengting, Wang Xianzhang, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Gongquan, Lin Kanghou, Du Chongyuan, Chu Fucheng, Yang Hu, Wu Xingya, Qi Shiying, Zang Qifang, Chen Lifu, Ye Xiufeng, Wang Yansong, Wu Tiecheng, Li Denghui, Zhu Qinglan, Xiong Xiling, Wang Zhuoran, Mi Chunlin, Wang Shuhan, Li Xien, Xiao Zhenying.

Our army has suffered a lot of losses, but after a year of bloody battles, we have dealt a lot of blows to the Japanese warlords. Shao Lizi Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning

Stating That a Method Must Be Determined to Relieve the Northwest

Will Return Home to Bury His Mother and Take a Rest

Shao Lizi, the chairman of the Gansu Provincial Government, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing yesterday morning at about 8 o'clock with his wife, Ms. Chuan Xuewen. He went to the hotel to rest, and in the afternoon, he went out by car to visit relatives and friends. In the evening, at 7 o'clock, he went to the Hua'an Hotel on Jing'an Temple Road to attend the meeting of the Fudan University Board of Directors, and returned to the hotel at about 10 o'clock. The Central News Agency reporter paid a special visit last night and inquired about the development of the Northwest and other issues. Shao replied in detail as follows:

The Development of the Northwest According to Shao, regarding the development of the Northwest, he has contributed three opinions to the central government during his trip to Beijing from Gansu. The first is to complete the Longhai Railway and reach Lanzhou directly. If we want to develop the Northwest, we must first improve the transportation in the Northwest. The more convenient the transportation, the faster the development of the Northwest. Therefore, we must follow Dr. Sun Yat-Sen's teachings, rush to build railways in the Northwest, and especially implement the central government's repeated resolutions to quickly complete the extension of the Longhai Road to Lanzhou. The second is to establish a Northwest Work Relief Committee to carry out road construction and water conservancy projects. The Northwest has suffered from natural disasters and banditry for years, and the local area has long been devastated. At present, if we want to develop the Northwest, we must first save the people of the Northwest. I hope that the central government will use the spirit of relieving the Yangtze River flood disaster in previous years to relieve the Northwest and establish a Northwest Work Relief Committee, and first improve the transportation in the two provinces of Shaanxi and Gansu. The third is to use the latest modern scientific methods and economic strength to conquer nature. I hope that comrades who go to the Northwest should do more practical work and create benefits for the people of the Northwest.

Contribution to the Shanghai Business Community Central's Opinion

Now, I have one more word to contribute to the financial and business communities in Shanghai. I have been to Gansu for nine months, and the impression the Northwest has given me is very deep, that is, the Northwest is indeed a bitter place, but the wealth of the Northwest is hidden underground. Anyone who wants to develop it must first have this understanding: the wealth of the Northwest is hidden underground, and the people of the Northwest are suffering because they have no power to develop it. I hope that the financial and business communities in Shanghai will actively go to develop it, but those who want to develop the Northwest must have the courage and adventurous spirit of the Northeast Volunteer Army, and learn from the Americans who developed western America and the Russians who developed Siberia, so that they can achieve success. At present, the reason why people in Shanghai dare not rashly go to develop the Northwest is that they are worried about the safety of investment. Although I dare not say that the politics of the Northwest is on the right track, commerce and politics have a causal and cyclical relationship. If commerce is not developed, politics will not be able to improve, and vice versa, the more developed commerce is, the faster the improvement of politics will be. Comparing the history of various cities in our country, we can believe my words. If people in Shanghai can go to develop the Northwest, then the politics of the Northwest can gradually improve, and the safety problem is not worth considering. The more powerful the investment of people in Shanghai to the Northwest, the more guaranteed the safety problem will be. This is what I can guarantee for the financial and business communities in Shanghai. Even in the current situation, if people in Shanghai go to develop the Northwest, there is no danger. If I have the opportunity, I plan to talk with the leaders of the financial and business communities in Shanghai, so that they can know the real situation of the Northwest and feel at ease to invest. The intention to resign can be expected to be dispelled. I have been running around for years

In all directions, my mother has passed away for seven or eight years, and has not yet been buried. Moreover, my health has not been good recently, and the doctor has advised me to rest and travel more. Therefore, I plan to stay in Shanghai for three or four days, and then return to my hometown of Shaoxing to bury my mother and take a rest. Then, the reporter asked Shao if his intention to resign from the chairmanship of Gansu Province had been dispelled. Shao told the reporter that although the central government has been trying to persuade him to stay, he still hopes that the central government will appoint someone more capable to preside over the government of Gansu. He has no power to develop Gansu Province, and it is more beneficial to the people of Gansu to report the situation in the Northwest and the ways to develop it to the central government than to preside over the government of Gansu. From the reporter's observation of Shao's intention, if the central government can have concrete measures to relieve Gansu Province, Shao's intention to resign can be expected to be dispelled.

The Formal Completion Of The Asian Cultural Association

New Building On Museum Road

According to the Chinese-language "North China Daily News," the new building of the Asian Cultural Association on Museum Road held its official opening ceremony yesterday evening (23rd) at 5 PM. First, President Bo Fangji welcomed the guests, and then Chief Engineer Pei'er presided over the ceremony and announced the opening. Then, Dr. Cai Yuanpei and Dr. Wu Liande gave speeches one after another. Finally, Mao Gen, on behalf of the association, thanked the donors, and said that the Chief Engineer Bureau and Wu Liande were the two pillars of the association. Among the 150,000 taels of construction funds for the new association building, the Chief Engineer Bureau allocated 50,000 taels, and Wu Liande donated 20,000 taels alone. As for the remaining donations, a total of 40,000 taels were raised, and there is still a shortfall of 40,000 taels. It is reported that the association is the North China Branch of the British Asian Cultural Association, and its main purpose is to study Asian culture. It was first established in 1857 and was called the Shanghai Literary and Scientific Association. In 1858, it was merged into the Asian Cultural Association. Ten years later, the British government allocated the existing site, and the association building was built three years later. After more than 60 years, it was dilapidated, so it raised funds for several years, and the construction was restarted in July two years ago. The construction was delayed due to the Shanghai War, and it was not completed until the beginning of this year. The new building has six floors and integrates Chinese and Western architectural techniques. The first floor is the auditorium, which is named after Wu Liande to commemorate him. The second floor is the library, the third and fourth floors are the museum, and the fifth floor is for the display of works of art.

Page 12

First Export of Soviet Steamer 7

Huge Shipment of Tea Bricks to Vladivostok

Measures for Chinese Citizens Going to Russia

Large Quantities of Timber Arrive

Since the resumption of Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations, the Soviet merchant fleet has resumed the Shanghai-Vladivostok route. Initially, chartered ships were used. Now, the fleet has officially dispatched ships to Shanghai. It has been several years since Soviet merchant ships came to China. The arrival of the "Losovsky" this time, which will return to Vladivostok, marks the first export of a Soviet steamer after the resumption of diplomatic ties. Sino-Soviet trade is gradually improving, and measures have been established for Chinese citizens going to Vladivostok. Details are recorded below:

Chinese Tea Transported to Russia

Chinese Tea, Sales in Russia

are substantial, especially tea bricks.

The outbound volume is large, often several thousand

tons. In the past, it was transported via the Chinese Eastern Railway to Russia. Now that the Northeast has been occupied by Japan, goods from Shanghai to Russia are all transported by sea. Since the resumption of Sino-Soviet diplomatic relations, Russia has come to China to purchase tea extensively. Tomorrow, the first regular Sino-Soviet steamer of the Soviet merchant fleet, the "Losovsky," will depart, carrying over four thousand tons of Chinese tea bricks, fully loaded, worth over a million yuan. This is the first large shipment of tea since the resumption of relations.

Chinese Citizens Going to Russia Before the resumption of diplomatic relations, Chinese citizens in the Soviet

Union were primarily in Vladivostok,

with several thousand

workers from Shandong province. The rest were mostly business operators. Many of them ceased operations and returned to China due to the country's taxation issues. There were very few Chinese in Vladivostok, and the entry restrictions were strict. Since the resumption of diplomatic relations, Chinese citizens going to Russia still require entry passports. However, before the Russian consulate in Shanghai is restored, an accommodating measure has been negotiated between our side and the Soviet authorities: Chinese citizens in Shanghai traveling to Vladivostok by ship must first obtain a passport from our Public Security Bureau, which is then forwarded to Dalian Bay to have it signed by the Russian consul stationed there, and returned to Shanghai. They can then board the ship to Vladivostok based on this passport. Without this passport, they will not be allowed to land.

Fixed Fares The Transportation Department of the Chinese Eastern Railway is the

general office in Shanghai managing the Soviet merchant fleet.

Commercial steamers traveling between China and Russia are all under the management of this office. As more Chinese citizens are traveling to Russia, fixed fares have been established for first, second, and third class passenger tickets on merchant ships traveling between Shanghai and Vladivostok. A first-class cabin from Shanghai to Vladivostok costs 100 yuan, and a third-class cabin from Shanghai to Vladivostok costs only 30 yuan. New regulations will be established after the official schedules for Sino-Russian passenger ships of the merchant fleet are determined.

Timber Arrives in Large Quantities Timber merchants in Shanghai have

placed orders for large quantities of timber

from the Soviet Union, and seven or eight batches

have already arrived successively, totaling over ten million feet. The shipment has not yet been completed. Now, another large batch of timber is being transported by the "Dao Yi" ship, which is scheduled to arrive at the port for unloading on the morning of the 27th, according to a telegram received yesterday.

Amid National Crisis

Duan's Painful Words

Refuses Birthday Celebrations, Doesn't Even Want to Hear the Word "Birthday"

According to Guowen News Agency, a person close to Duan Zhiquan said yesterday that March 4th (the ninth day of the second lunar month) is Duan's 69th birthday. Acquaintances in Shanghai, such as Yu Qiaqing, Zhang Yuejun, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, and Zhang Xiaolin, planned to initiate a public celebration, but Duan politely declined. Duan believes that today the nation is nearly in a perilous state. It's like being careless and getting robbed. One should be busy putting out the fire and defending against robbers, and should not have the leisure to engage in leisurely activities. Moreover, he has never celebrated a birthday in his life. As for today, he not only does not want to celebrate a birthday, but doesn't even want to hear the word "birthday." He will also refuse to accept any birthday screens, couplets, poems, or the like. Those who understand him will understand, and so on.

After arriving in Shanghai, Duan Qirui first temporarily resided in the World Society on Ferguson Road. Later, he found the former residence of Chen Diaoyuan at No. 1487 on Avenue Joffre and plans to move in soon. A reporter from the Shen Shi Telegraph Agency met with Xu Shiying yesterday, who said that Duan is scheduled to move into his new residence today (the 25th). In addition, Duan has recently suffered from a mild abdominal illness and has engaged Wang Zhongqi, a traditional Chinese medicine practitioner from his hometown of Anhui, for treatment. He rarely receives guests. The Ministry of Communications Issues a Circular Urging Caution in Employing Seamen

Those Without Certificates Are Not Allowed to Be Hired

Severe Punishment Will Be Imposed If Violations Are Discovered

Recently, after the accidents involving the "Xin Ning," "Tai Da Yun," and other ships, which resulted in the drowning deaths of large numbers of people, the Ministry of Communications, out of concern for the safety of lives, has decided that seamen without nautical knowledge and experience and those who have not been examined and certified by the Ministry will not be allowed to be employed. A circular was issued yesterday to Shanghai, ordering the shipping industry association to comply. The original text is as follows: Circular on Compliance Matters: It has been clearly stipulated in the Commercial Ship Officer Certificate Regulations and Article 3 of the Provisional Regulations for Seamen Management promulgated by the Ministry that seamen must not serve without holding certificates. This is because the quality of seamen's skills is related to the safety of navigation. Those who have not been examined and qualified by the Ministry and given certificates can hardly be competent. Recently, there have been frequent incidents and accidents involving ships on the rivers and seas. The reasons are complex, but one of the reasons is the employment of seamen without certificates. This should be stopped to ensure safety. In addition to separate orders, this is also ordered to the association to forward to all shipping companies to comply. In the future, all seamen who have not obtained certificates from this Ministry are not allowed to be hired. If violations are discovered, they will be severely investigated and punished without leniency. This order.

Water Cutoff Dispute Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Council Board of Directors will definitely discuss the water supply issue at length at next Wednesday's meeting. The British-owned Shanghai Waterworks Company, in order to prepare for coping with the situation, has also scheduled a meeting on the 27th (next Monday) to discuss how to deal with the environment and resolve the dispute. The Shuncheng Lane Refusal to Cut Off Water Committee yesterday sent representatives Zhou Binzhang and others to submit letters to various agencies and important organizations to petition. The original text reads: Petition for cutting off water and starvation, requesting to save lives. Since the water supply to Shuncheng Lane and other areas in Yangshupu was cut off on February 16, residents have been unable to cook, causing widespread panic. Shanghai is densely populated with Chinese factories, and residents are dense, with workers making up the majority. Their knowledge is very limited. If this continues for a long time, unfortunate tragedies may occur. Therefore, residents have organized the "Shanghai Pudong Shuncheng Lane and Other Refusal to Cut Off Water Committee" to appeal to all parties. Therefore, this petition is submitted for your consideration, requesting prompt relief, which would be a great virtue.

The 6th District Branch of the Citizens' Federation yesterday sent

a letter to the Shanghai Chinese Ratepayers' Association General Federation of Citizens' Federation, stating: We respectfully report that recently, tenants Sheng Xinru, Qiu Jialiang, Chen Baoxing, Zhang Hechun, Chen Xintian, etc. from Jingqing Lane on Xihua De Road wrote to us stating that since the water company cut off the water supply on the morning of the 20th, they have been unable to obtain water and have had to elect Qiu Jialiang and others as representatives to negotiate with the Shanghai Municipal Council to temporarily use the Taiping tap on the roadside at the entrance of the lane for emergency use. As a result, those fetching water all day are extremely crowded, causing disputes and fights. The area is densely populated and the danger is extremely high, making tragedies difficult to avoid. Therefore, they came to the association to request filing for record, respectfully requesting your association's assistance and a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Council stating that if a tragedy occurs in that area due to the water cutoff, the water company should bear full responsibility. Therefore, they request to maintain the previous situation and hope that the original state will be restored to avoid disputes and maintain peace. Accordingly, we hereby send a letter for your reference and handling. Truly a public matter.

Estonian Independence Day

A Grand Celebration Banquet Held by Estonians

Yesterday marked the 15th anniversary of the declaration of independence of Estonia, a country on the Baltic coast of Europe. Estonians in Shanghai gathered at the Astor House Hotel at 8:30 PM for a grand celebration banquet. Estonia is one of the newly emerging small countries after the European War. Its establishment is relatively recent. Previously, due to its strategic location between major powers, it had been under the control of Germanic, Danish, Swedish, and Russian countries since the 13th century, but it retained its autonomous status. After the European War, it, along with Finland, Lithuania, and Latvia, separated from Russia and formed a democratic republic government. Various ethnic minorities in the country, such as Russians, Germans, Swedes, and Jews, enjoy full rights. The authorities pay particular attention to education and culture, so there are no illiterates in the country. The people are fond of music, and a national singing festival is held every four years. The number of participants, including hymn singers and musicians, has reached 16,000, which can be said to be a grand occasion. There are a total of 117 Estonians in Shanghai, of whom 17 hold positions such as ship captains.

Forms Sightseeing Tour to the U.S.

Exhibition to Host Various Sectors Tomorrow

The Preparatory Committee for China's participation in the Chicago Expo held another regular meeting yesterday and resolved to form a sightseeing tour to the U.S. and host an exhibition. Tomorrow, it will host various sectors. Details are recorded separately below.

Committee held a regular meeting of its preparatory committee at the exhibition venue.

More than ten people, including He Bingxian, Cai Wuji, Zha Baohua, Zhang Xianglin, and Miao Zhongxiu, attended. He Bingxian chaired the meeting. First, Cai Wuji reported on the opening of the exhibition. Then, several important matters were resolved, including the resolution to invite various sectors in Shanghai to form a sightseeing tour to the U.S. in June when the Chicago Expo opens to appreciate the grand occasion of the conference. The expenses for travel, accommodation, and meals will be self-funded, estimated to cost about US$600-700. Zhang Xianglin, director of the secretariat, has been appointed to plan everything.

Holding a Tea Party In appreciation of the enthusiastic support from various sectors

for this exhibition, it has been decided to hold a grand tea party at the venue at 3:00 PM

on the afternoon of the 26th to express gratitude. Over 500 invitations have been sent out, and there will be a grand occasion at that time. In addition, after the chairmen of various groups were appointed the day before, Chairman Cai Yuanpei is scheduled to invite the chairmen of various groups this afternoon to discuss the review methods. After the Fierce Battle Began

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Sends a Telegram to Zhang Tang

Urging Perseverance and Self-Control, Not to Be Discouraged by Small Setbacks

Yesterday, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to Zhang Xueliang in Beiping and Tang Yulin in Rehe. The original text reads: To Acting Committee Member Zhang of the Beiping Military Branch and Chairman Tang of Chengde, please forward to the soldiers at the front: We previously received a telegram, expressing loyalty and patriotism. We are deeply moved. The battle has just begun, and there will be times of advantage and disadvantage. We hope that you will persevere and maintain self-control, not be discouraged by small setbacks, and donate funds to repay the country. The people of the whole country share this sentiment. Do not let the generals bear the difficulties alone. Respectfully, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce

Issues an Open Letter to Merchants Nationwide

Today, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued an open letter to chambers of commerce nationwide, stating: Since the September 18th Incident, we have lost three provinces with our hands tied due to repeated concessions, creating an unprecedented painful history of opening up the sea border. The whole country laments this. Although patriots and people of noble aspirations in the three provinces have risen up and fought the enemy, their efforts have not saved the critical situation in the three provinces. This is because foreign wars require concentrated strength and national unity. Relying solely on the people to fight on their own results in a scattered situation and weak backing, which is not enough to resist the full force of a strong enemy. For more than a year, the government has been focusing all its energy on diplomacy, hoping to recover lost territories without war. Who knew that the enemy's flames would grow stronger and their plans would become more urgent? They plan to include the Rehe region in their territory and seize it, plotting to gradually divide and cause the sinking of China. Therefore, the government, unable to bear it any longer, authorized the military authorities in North China to concentrate troops and make a last stand. Dean Song also made trips to Beiping and Chengde to raise military funds and comfort the soldiers. At the same time, it telegraphed the League of Nations, expressing its attitude. All these situations can be said to have broken the stagnant and contradictory situation of the past year and opened up a tragic and fierce path from now on. The people and the government are in the same leaky boat and cannot simply maintain an attitude of watching the fire from across the river and stand purely in a position of criticism and observation. Therefore, if the government has not decided on a major plan for resisting the war, the people should urge it. If the government is determined to carry out the anti-Japanese campaign, the people should fully support it. The actions of the invading country are the culmination of its decades of policy. The mobilization of 60 million people should be met with the efforts of our 400 million people. We must save on clothing and food, endure hardship, and store every bit of resources to support the military and resist Japan, so that the morale is always fresh and the front line is stable, which may save the critical situation and make the invaders aware. We hope that the government will be like Wen Tianxiang, and we must first hope that the people can be like Han Buxi, destroying their homes to relieve the national crisis. Merchants are at the forefront of this. We are willing to fulfill our responsibility with a spirit of not shirking responsibility. National sentiments and the consolidation of the country are the duties that our country's merchants should fulfill today. Let us encourage each other.

Eight Types of Public Bonds Will Be Drawn for Redemption

Scheduled for March 10 at the Bankers' Association

Regarding the issued public bonds, the Ministry of Finance will draw eight types for redemption next month: (1) Austrian Indemnity Guaranteed, 1914 Treasury Bond, 9th Redemption; (2) Republic of China 7% Public Bond, 13th Redemption; (3) Republic of China 1925 Short-Term Public Bond, 13th Redemption; (4) National Government Military Public Bond, 9th Redemption; (5) Rehabilitation Public Bond, 12th Redemption; (6) Republic of China 1928 Financial Short-Term Public Bond, 9th Redemption; (7) Republic of China 1929 Disaster Relief Public Bond, 11th Redemption; (8) Republic of China 1928 Customs Duty Public Bond, 9th Public Bond Redemption. The drawing of the above eight types of public bonds is scheduled for 10:00 AM on February 10 at the Bankers' Association on Hong Kong Road. If the drawn numbers match, except for the 1914 Treasury Bond, all payments will be made by the Bank of Communications, the Bank of China, and the Central Bank on March 20.

Dispute over Heavy Loads in the Rice Industry

The Party and Government Negotiated and Agreed on a Solution Yesterday

The strike by rice transporters has continued for three days and has not yet been resolved. The situation is very serious. The Party and government organs in this city negotiated a solution yesterday and scheduled a meeting for all relevant rice industry groups to attend and mediate. The details are recorded separately below.

Negotiating a Solution Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, He Yuanming from the Civil Movement Section of the Municipal Party Committee and Zhou Minggang from the Fourth Section of the Social Affairs Bureau negotiated a solution. They immediately decided: (1) Implement level measures and funnels; (2) Switch to using scales. The rice industry groups and transporters will be ordered to follow the method adopted after voting.

Scheduled Voting The Party and government organs, in order to solicit opinions from rice industry groups, measure associations, transporters, etc. on the adoption of level measures and funnels or the switch to using scales, have specifically scheduled a joint meeting on the morning of the 28th of this month at 10:00 AM to be attended by representatives from the four groups: the Rice Industry Association, the Rice Shop Association, the Measure Association, and the United Association of Rice Transporters. They have also sent letters to the Measurement and Calibration Institute to send personnel to attend and participate in the meeting to provide their views for voting.

Rice Merchants

Using Six-Dou Measuring Instruments

The Food Commission Submits a Request for Temporary Approval

After the new municipal measure was adopted in this city, the capacity was reduced compared to the Shanghai measure. All commission fees, miscellaneous fees, etc. should be reduced accordingly. Some rice merchants have also requested to use six-dou measuring instruments. This was proposed at the 39th meeting of the Food Commission. Before the new municipal measure is adopted in customs and rice producing areas, it is proposed to temporarily allow the use of six-dou measuring instruments. For other commission fees, miscellaneous fees, etc., except for those calculated by bag, they should still be proportionally reduced. It has been reported to the municipal government for submission to the Ministry of Industry for record. After the municipal government received the report, in addition to ordering a reply, it has also forwarded it to the Ministry of Industry for record.
