Free Talk

Lessons from One Civil and One Military 27

— Yu Dafu

China has recently received lessons from two foreign mentors, one civil and one military. The civil one, of course, is that oily-tongued old man, George Bernard Shaw. In Beijing, he said to reporters: "One strange characteristic of the Chinese is their incredible politeness and friendliness towards all foreigners, but among themselves, they are always so impolite and always fighting." He also said that the Great Wall is no different from an ordinary low wall.

The military one is the Japanese imperialists' cannons and airplanes that recently invaded Jehol. These cannons and airplanes are also laughing and saying to the Chinese: "You Chinese are so polite to foreigners and so impolite to your own people. You have given up tens of thousands of miles of the Northeast, and now this Jehol, after you get your war bonds and collect your support and慰勞 money, you will have to give it up again. The Great Wall was originally built to defend against foreign invasions, but now it has become a fortress and boundary line for foreigners. It can be considered a defense project built by the Chinese for foreigners."

On the one hand, thinking of the wars in Shandong, Sichuan, and Guizhou during the so-called national crisis, one cannot help but admire the accuracy of the lessons from these two foreign mentors. In the end, I can only copy two old poems and change them to praise the progress of my great Chinese nation.

Revised Book of Songs: Brothers fight at the wall, inviting external insults.

Copied poem mocking Li Hongzhang and Weng Tonghe: Fortunately, Xiang Hefei makes the world thin, the Grand Council of Changshu makes the common people barren.

Revised poem from the past praising the Great Wall: Qin built the Great Wall like an iron prison, at that time who knew how much labor it would take, pitifully on the third night of the first month, giving it away to others to use as trenches.

Hometown 28

— Li Huiying

Like everyone who wanders outside has their own hometown, I also have my own hometown.

My hometown is neither a famous city nor a scenic spot. On the contrary, it is just a secluded little village. It is heavily surrounded on three sides by the remaining veins of Changbai Mountain, and on the other side it is close to the Yima River. This is a not-so-large valley mouth and a not-so-small plain, with mountains, water, and fertile fields, making it a very good farm, making it always envied and praised by the nearby farmers.

In winter and spring, the fields and mountain peaks are all covered with a thick layer of white snow, and the river water is also frozen with a thick layer of solid ice. At the end of spring, the snow gradually melts, the ice gradually disappears, and yellow grass is exposed everywhere. Then, green buds sprout, and the mountains and valleys, as well as the vast plains, are full of pleasing green; then, willow catkins fly, and it is time to start sowing. At this time, countless people are cultivating the fields, and flowers of various colors are blooming in the mountains and fields; then, the weather warms up, it gets hot, until autumn, harvesting, and it gets cold again, and there are many days. This is the climate of the year. People follow the changes of nature, calmly doing their own work, and this kind of life has been going on day after day for more than ninety years.

But in recent years, everything is obviously different from before. For example, land rent is increased, taxes are increased, bandits often rob, prices are more expensive year by year, and local products are gradually reduced, and finally disappear; everything used is foreign goods; the agricultural products harvested in a year, after being sold, not only cannot save some money as before, but become unusually difficult,………… These, even if people don't know what's going on, or don't think carefully about the reason, there is no doubt that their lives have fallen from stability into an inexplicable hardship. My hometown, although just a secluded village, finally cannot escape this general phenomenon of rural destruction.

However, if it were just like this, they could still live hard by relying on their own labor: but now? Now everything is over, and they can't even live a life of hardship. Poor hometown, now it has been completely destroyed; under the planes and cannons of Japanese imperialism, it has been burned and burned, and all the houses, fields, livestock and property are gone, and now only a devastated ruin remains. Ah丨 Jinjiatun, my dear hometown丨 If one day I can return to your arms, where will I go to find the remains of my old home?

Plunder Marriage among Savage Races 29

— Li Jianfeng

Plunder marriage has gradually decreased with the progress of human civilization, but this custom is still prevalent among uncivilized savage tribes.

The American Indian tribes still perform this tragicomedy everywhere today. Battles often occur between these tribes: the mounted Indians of Patagonia and the canoe-riding Indian tribes often have battles between individuals and battles between tribes. When they win, they kill the men and kidnap the women. In the tribes of the Amazon and Orinoco, slightly north of these two tribes, except for a portion influenced by Christianity, the rest are still constantly fighting each other, often capturing the women of the other side to use for bearing children. The Indians in the Caribbean region are divided into many small tribes or family groups, with each tribe or group having about forty to fifty people. These tribes often have conflicts due to different languages that they cannot understand. The winning tribe not only carries out large-scale massacres, but also takes the killed people to fill their stomachs丨 However, these killed and eaten people are all men, and the women are usually kept and taken back to be wives. In Australian savage society, this trend of plunder marriage is more harmful than in the above-mentioned regions, and the methods of plunder are also more cruel. Because there are more men than women in Australia, men in various tribes simply rarely get sexual satisfaction. When they need women, the only way is to plunder. They often secretly watch the movements of the woman they love, and when the woman is not wary, they suddenly run over and stun her with a stick, then twist her hair and drag her to the nearby forest. When she regains consciousness, they force her to go to his home together to carry out what they call married life. And the woman's family does not feel resentful about this cruel behavior, because they are the same. When the opportunity comes, they will also commit the same atrocities against other people's women. Readers may be very surprised to see these words, but these are all savage peoples, which is still excusable. If I tell you that even the newest countries like the Soviet Union still have this habit, wouldn't that be even more shocking? Originally, there are some Caucasian people in Russia who still regard this kind of marriage as commonplace. They often snatch women at night and put them on horses. If they are chased, then the horses, weapons, and everything else will be confiscated. If they succeed, then the bride will live with him. This custom of plunder marriage is also popular among the Letts and Uchi people north of Estonia. The most interesting are the Uchi people, who often snatch women when the women's parents are working in the fields or sleeping in the house.

Plunder marriage relies entirely on the man's unilateral will to grab a woman to satisfy his own desires, completely ignoring the woman's love, interests, and even sexual desires. This can be said to be the most savage and cruel form of marriage. In the 20th century, the existence of plunder marriage can be said to be a disgrace to humanity!

A Black Woman's Quest for God (XI) 30

— Written by George Bernard Shaw, Translated by Yi Xian

[Brains!] the shortsighted one said, as if he could hardly believe his ears. [You must be a very ignorant girl,] he chuckled. [Do you not know that a scientist is all brains from head to foot?]

[Tell that to the fishes,] the black girl said. [Tell me again. Have you ever considered the effect of your experiments on the spirits and characters] of other people? Is it worth while to lose your own soul and corrupt everybody elses for the sake of discovering something about dogs' spittle?]

[You are talking nonsense,] said the shortsighted one. [Can you prove the existence of this organ you call a soul on the operating table or in the dissecting room? Can you reproduce in the laboratory this process you call corruption?] [By tapping with my] [Nobberkeleigh,] the black girl said, [I can change a living soul into a dead body with no soul in it. Then you can see the difference and appreciate it. And when people do wicked things to corrupt their] souls you see the difference then too.]

[I have seen people die; but I have never seen them corrupting their souls,] said the shortsighted one.

[But you have seen them go to the devil, havnt you?] said the black girl. [You are going to the devil yourself, are you not?] [That is an insult; a most extreme personal insult,] said the shortsighted one loftily. [I leave you.]

So he went his way, thinking only of how to make a dog climb a tree to prove scientifically that he could climb a tree himself; and the black girl went her way until she came to a little hill, on the top of which stood a huge cross, guarded by a Roman soldier with a long lance. Now the priest, who had found the same queer joy in crucifying terror that she had found in breaking her own heart and the hearts of her lovers, had, in spite of all her lessons, made the black girl hate the cross, because it was a great pity that Jesus had not lived to a ripe old age of wisdom and died peacefully without suffering, and so could not protect his granddaughters (she imagined that Jesus had at least twenty promising black granddaughters) against the selfishness and tyranny of their parents. Therefore, she turned her head away from the cross with an expression of marked disgust, just as the Roman soldier rushed at her with his lance and roared, [Slave, kneel before the emblem and instrument of Roman justice, Roman law, Roman order, and] Roman peace, et cetera.]

But the black girl avoided the lance and swung her [Nobberkeleigh] with such effect on the back of his neck that he collapsed, unable to put his legs together again. [That is the emblem and instrument of slavey and all that is excellent,] said the black girl, showing him the [Nobberkeleigh. [How do you like it?] [Ugh!] groaned the soldier. [A hero done in by a black female dog! The end of the world has come.] And he stopped struggling, and lay on the ground crying like a child.

He had recovered before she was far away; but he was a Roman soldier and could not leave his post to indulge his feelings. The last she saw of him before the edge of the little hill cut off their view of one another was his fist shaking at her; and the last she heard from him need not be repeated here.

Her next adventure was by a well, where she stopped to drink, and suddenly saw a man sitting beside it, whom she had not noticed before. Just as she was about to scoop up some water with her hand, he produced a cup from somewhere and said,

[Take this and drink, in remembrance of me.]

[Thank you, Sir,] she said, and drank immediately. [Thank you very much.]

Random Words from Qu Lu 31

— Zizhan

(8) The Hair-Cutting Movement in the Late Qing Dynasty

Men wore braids like factory tails, and women bound their small feet to be called golden lotuses. When Europeans and Americans first saw these strange-looking Chinese people, they were all surprised, or even ridiculed and despised them. This is where the idea of cutting braids and unbinding feet in the late Qing Dynasty came from. The hair-cutting movement originated from overseas students and overseas Chinese, and many new scholars in the mainland also followed suit. Overseas students with revolutionary ideas often cut their braids, and overseas Chinese who did not want to return to China also cut their braids. Although the Qing court initially banned it, it eventually had no choice. Zhang Taiyan has a poem written in prison for Zou Rong:

Zou Rong, my younger brother, with disheveled hair, went down to the continent.

Quickly cut off the braids with scissors, dried beef is the throat.

The hero has entered prison, and the world is also sad in autumn.

When life is about to end, we must join hands, the universe is only two ends.

This poem is not included in Zhang's collection, but only appeared in the Zhejiang Chao B number thirty years ago. Zhang's thesis is based on the Wei and Jin Dynasties, despising the Qi and Liang Dynasties and below, so there are no near-style poems in the collection. Now that there is this poem, it is even more precious and unusual. The poem describes his and Zou Rong's spirit, which is most representative of the so-called revolutionary heroes of that time, and the only characteristic of these heroes is that they can use [quick scissors to cut off their braids.] In the second year of Xuantong, Wu Tingfang, the former minister to the United States, submitted a memorial requesting that hair be cut and clothes not be changed, which roughly said: When I was an envoy to the Americas, I met with overseas Chinese and saw that they had cut their braids and changed to Western suits, eight or nine out of ten. Some who have not cut them off, also coil them high on their heads, hidden and closed tightly, fearing that people will know. They all say that drooping braids are often ridiculed by foreigners, and even given various unflattering names, sometimes even teased by women and children. Moreover, it is inconvenient for them to work and they get their clothes dirty, which is even more criticized. Moreover, with machine manufacturing and factories everywhere, there are often reports of people getting into danger because of their braids. He also said: Since the eastward spread of European customs, the residents of the mainland, except for officials and gentry, all students, scholars, men and women, workers, merchants, and farmers, have cut off their long hair for the sake of convenience in their daily lives, everywhere. People belong to the same country and live in the same country, but they wear different clothes and have different systems, as if they were from Chu and Yue. This is truly rare in the world, and it is also something that those who observe the country and collect customs are surprised by. Moreover, as the trend of the times becomes newer and newer, their number will only increase. Even strict laws and severe prohibitions will not be able to stop it. As the saying goes, change or not change, it will change. Why not change it ourselves, and still have something to encourage the spirit of innovation from top to bottom? The memorial was not answered. A year later, there was the Guangzhou March 29th Uprising. Many party members died, but among those buried in Huanghuagang, there were also those who were not party members but had cut off their braids. At that time, the Hong Kong Chinese Clothing Hair-Cutting Association had more than ten thousand members, all of whom were uneasy and considered Guangzhou a place to be feared.

Page 17

Spring and Autumn

Bridge and Old Man Zhanlu 32

— Zhanlu

丨Cutting the Iron Bridge丨

The relationship between bridges and old people, everyone knows, there is Huang Shigong who dropped his shoe on the bridge, this kind of familiar old story, of course, there is no need to repeat it. Now, what is mentioned is not a story but a current event, the bridge, not the one above the mound, is an iron bridge, the old man, not Huang Shigong, is the old man Huang Wei: the relationship between the bridge and the old man is not that the old man Huang Shigong dropped his shoe on the bridge, but that the old man Huang Wei cut the rope on the bridge.

The rope-cutting ceremony for a new bridge opening to traffic has the same importance as the bottle-throwing ceremony for a new ship launching: the only difference is that the bottle-throwing ceremony is suitable for women with beautiful faces, while the rope-cutting ceremony is suitable for old men with white hair. Guangzhou recently held a Qiying meeting, with two people over the age of one hundred, a man named Huang Wei, and a woman named Deng Huangshi, who are highly respected by local people. Recently, because of the Haizhu Iron Bridge, which has been under construction for more than two years, a driving ceremony was held on the 15th of this month. A pair of golden scissors was made by the Mackdon Company, which built the bridge, for the purpose of cutting the rope for the bridge opening; the Social Bureau also sent a letter to the oldest Qiying in middle age, Huang Wei, who has many children and grandchildren, to hold the knife to perform the rope-cutting ceremony. Then, Huang Wei and fourteen other old people led the way across the bridge, followed by military and political leaders, while music was played and cannons were fired, announcing the completion of the ceremony. This is truly an unprecedented grand event.

Since the call to overthrow the old and decaying has become louder, [old people and yellowed pearls are worthless,] of course, everyone recognizes them as outdated figures: Guangzhou held a Qiying meeting, and also invited a centenarian to be the pioneer to cross the bridge; the old men and old women were in the limelight, to put it nicely, it is respecting the old and respecting seniority, to put it badly, it is reversing the wheel of the times.

Rubber Band 33

— Baihe

丨Be Careful Not to Snap It丨

In the joint declaration of Zhang Taiyan and Ma Xiangbo, it is said that Japan's rubber band should be retracted from Korea. The three characters [Rubber Band] are used very meaningfully.

Men and women, old and young, all comrades who do not tie up their trouser legs, please lift your trouser legs to your knees, remain silent for three minutes, and think carefully: are the garter belts, each occupying a piece on your two hairy calves, Japanese products? Within these Japanese garter belts, is there a trace of rubber band?

Indeed, this is a rubber band. This kind of rubber band, if it is not woven into cotton fabric, can be stretched to several times its original length.

Japan's original territory is like a narrow and long rubber band. Since it occupied Ryukyu and Taiwan, and swallowed Korea and Liaodong, Japan's rubber band has been stretched very long. After the European War, it took over the German-owned South Pacific Islands, stretching the rubber band several times longer. However, since seizing the Northeast, although the rubber band has been stretched somewhat again, various countries have begun to interfere, and instability has gradually emerged within Japan. This is like a rubber band, although stretched long, has exceeded its ability to withstand the force, and is showing signs of breaking.

Although a rubber band can be stretched long, once it breaks and shrinks into two small segments, it cannot maintain its original length. Therefore, stretching a rubber band, although it seems like a fun trick, is actually a very dangerous thing. A three-inch-long rubber band can only be used for three inches. If you insist on using a three-inch rubber band for three feet, then once it breaks, it cannot even be used for three inches. What is the point of that?

Japan's rubber band has now been stretched to the point of breaking. If it does not let go, once it breaks, everything will be over, and even the original length cannot be maintained, as it will already be divided into two segments.

Zhang and Ma advise Japan to retract the rubber band from Korea, which is indeed the right medicine for the problem. However, one does not give up until reaching the Yellow River; if the rubber band does not break, how can Japan be willing to stop?

Remaining Words on the Liu Case 34

— Jun

The tragic death of Liu Yusheng, the chief writer of the Jiangsheng Daily in Zhenjiang, is a major topic of discussion in the city and known throughout the country. During his lifetime, Liu had a ten-year friendship with Yan Fusun due to their shared literary interests. Last autumn, when Liu was imprisoned, Liu's relatives and friends all ran around to rescue him. Liu's family once consulted the oracle in a gourd, receiving the two characters [口] [合]. Yan immediately deduced, "The character 口 clearly represents a tiger's mouth, taking the character [人] and sending it into the tiger's mouth creates the character [囚] (prisoner). A person placed within this airtight mouth can no longer escape, and the outcome is likely very dangerous. Look at this character [合], it is clearly an incomplete character [命] (life). A life character that is interrupted, is nothing other than a broken life!" Madam Liu, a weak woman, wept bitterly upon hearing this interpretation. Several months later, unexpectedly, Liu's fate tragically corresponded to the oracle in the gourd. Alas! Fate is predetermined, what more can be said?

Saving the Nation with a Magic Weapon 35

— Xu Yu

丨[Ten Thousand Divinely Blessed Yellow Bags]丨

During the Qing Dynasty, Gangyi, because he hated foreign devils, prepared to fight them, so he trained some soldiers called [Tiger Spirit Battalion]: taking the meaning that [Tigers] can eat [Sheep] and [Spirits] can subdue [Ghosts]. Furthermore, by reciting incantations, bullets could not penetrate the flesh. By casting spells, [foreign devils] would be killed by flying sand and stones. As a result, although the incantations were useless, they did indeed subdue many [ghosts], causing a disturbance. At the time, the higher-class Chinese people were not saddened by the failure, but rather blamed them for being too foolish, and not being respectable in their interactions with the [scientific] foreign adults, so they called them [Boxer Rebellion]. [Boxer] means bare hands: concealing those broadswords, spears, incantations, shields, and other [national treasures] [divine weapons]. [Rebellion] was an excuse for the government to absolve itself of responsibility. Moreover, it could be used to [suppress bandits], and [suppressing bandits] could be used to appease foreigners. Since it was both [Boxer] and [Rebellion], it was naturally appropriate to add [Disturbance]. However, [times change], Mr. Sun Yat-sen praised them as a manifestation of national revolutionary consciousness. The wronged souls in hell finally had a chance to ascend. However, the subtle distinctions in terminology truly make people believe in the iron rule that [if the name is not correct, then the words will not be proper]. For example, looking at today's newspaper, there is another piece of news similar to the above. The original text is as follows: (20th, Beiping Telegram) The Most Venerable Quanhe donates and manufactures ten thousand divinely blessed yellow bags to be gifted to the frontline armies.

Now the Japanese devils have already invaded Rehe, and the whole country is united against the enemy. Monks are also citizens of China, and their patriotic hearts should not lag behind. However, the [aviation to save the nation] advocated by various sectors is inconsistent with [unscientific] teachings. Therefore, there is the [saving the nation with a magic weapon] of [divinely blessed yellow bags]. The [Spirit] in [Divinely Blessed Yellow Bags] and the [Spirit] in [Tiger Spirit Battalion] both take the meaning of subduing ghosts. The three characters [Tiger Spirit Battalion] only imply attack and not defense, a lesson learned from the overturned cart in front. Therefore, [Blessing] is used. By both subduing ghosts and blessing oneself, one can be said to know oneself and one's enemy, and thus be able to win every battle.

And saving the nation can also spread the teaching at the same time; this is secondary. Therefore, recalling the anti-Japanese war in Songhu last spring, female students from various places all donated military uniforms, clothing, trousers, and the like, and some even personally embroidered characters such as [Wishing you victory] [True Man], greatly boosting the morale of the army. But compared to [divinely blessed yellow bags], it is far behind!

The Philosophy of Money 36

— Yu Sijin

丨One of the Things I Write When I Think of Them丨

Money, it is money that makes people live, and it is also money that makes people die.

Capitalists rack their brains to exploit the poor for money, and the proletariat desperately resists, isn't that also for money? Cities are created by money, and at the same time, the vagrants in cities are also created by money. Destroying the countryside is even more the magic of money.

The soul of the saver is entrusted to money. The soul of the moneyless is also spinning around in money.

Wanting to become an official is wanting money; originally, wanting to do any career, simply put, is wanting money.

Money is easily exchanged for guns, but guns are exchanged for money by luck.

People say that people should not be manipulated by money, but how many are not manipulated by money?

As the times evolve and material civilization advances, money becomes more useful, and its magic becomes greater.

Nine out of ten old women go to temples to offer incense for money. Whether one's status in society is high or low fundamentally depends on money.

With money, one can go to university and study abroad, buy doctoral and bachelor's degrees, eat big meals and ride in cars in the city; without money, one stays at home, illiterate, the agricultural and forestry economy goes bankrupt, and one comes to the city to wander.

Only money is worthy of the title of [omnipotent doctor]. The saying is indeed true: with money by your side, you walk in the middle of the road; without money by your side, you walk like a plague insect.

Novel

The Landowner 37

— Qin Shouou

倭子, 倭子 means 倭寇 (Japanese pirates). Because Chongming is an island, and the defending troops are particularly weak, therefore, in the few years before the imminent downfall of the Ming Dynasty, Japanese pirates began to sail across the sea in small boats, relying on their sharp Japanese swords, to rob and plunder in groups: since the officials could not protect the people, the people had no choice but to rise up and resist automatically. The landowner was one of the most ardent advocates of resistance. In the past five years, he had already commanded his sons and the villagers of one village to defeat the Japanese pirates twice.

[Good! Old man! Remember this! In three years we will come back for revenge, and we will kill your entire village, leaving not a single dog or chicken, to vent our anger!] When the Japanese pirates were defeated for the second time, and the landowner led the masses to chase them all the way to the seaside, one of the Japanese pirates, who had already boarded the boat, pointed his Japanese sword at the landowner, gnashing his teeth, and making this vow.

Past events proved that what this Japanese pirate said was not a facetious threat, because the Japanese pirates are the most vicious and most bestial beings, and they list killing as part of their family education, especially being brave in revenge. The landowner also believed that his words would be realized one day, so after that pacification, his heart was extremely uneasy: however, he was not afraid, nor did he want to abandon his home and flee, he only worked hard to train his sons and villagers, preparing for a great slaughter every day.

Therefore, Little Ling's father used fighting the Japanese pirates to inspire his son; Little Ling listened, and also worked especially hard, wishing he could immediately grow hundreds of pounds of strength, so that he could stab holes in the chests of the Japanese pirates with his spear.

The setting sun gradually dimmed, but the people practicing martial arts on the field were not decreasing; the landowner raised his white head, looked at the newly rising crescent moon, and let out a smug smile.

Suddenly, a burst of noisy human voices arose outside the forest, interspersed with the crying of women and children.

[Landowner! Disaster has struck!] Immediately, a strong young man, protected by six fierce dogs, ran in as if flying. [This time is not like before! Landowner!]

What should be done!

The people practicing martial arts stopped their activities and gathered around the landowner and the messenger. [What disaster? Explain clearly!] the landowner urged.

[Japanese pirates! Japanese pirates! Japanese pirates everywhere! I really don't know how many have come,] the messenger shouted as if he were crazy. (3)

Children's Paradise

Chicken 38

The sexagenary cycle for this year is Guiyou, and You belongs to the chicken. I will talk about chickens.

What did chickens evolve from? According to research, the ancestors of chickens originally lived in the wilderness, living the same lives as wild chickens. Later, they were captured by humans and raised at home, gradually shedding their wild nature. If we observe them in the wilderness of present-day India, Siam, the Malay Peninsula, and so on, we can determine that the ancestors of chickens were indeed wild chickens.

Before clocks were invented, people relied entirely on the crowing of chickens to calculate the time, the so-called first watch chicken, second watch chicken... fifth watch chicken, which we often see in myths and novels. However, the species of chickens can be divided into more than five hundred types according to the size of their bodies and the color of their plumage. Among them, the most precious is the long-tailed chicken, whose tail feathers can be as long as seven meters. As for the most prolific egg-laying chicken, it is a short-tailed, white-colored Xiumo species. The incubation period for hens is approximately three weeks. Nowadays, artificial incubation (electric temperature incubator) is mostly used in various countries, and each time it can incubate 10,000 to 20,000 eggs, so the breeding of chickens has increased more and more in recent years.

The Wonders of Numbers 39

Gentlemen, today I will write down two ingenious ways of calculating numbers for everyone to see, and other methods can be deduced similarly. For example, starting from one times nine plus two below, it becomes a very interesting equation.

Multiplying by Nine to Get a Hundred 40

— Bing Yu

For example, nine times ten is ninety, times eleven is ninety-nine, times twelve is one hundred and eight, but it is very difficult to multiply and get exactly one hundred. Now if you multiply four nines together, that is 99, which is exactly one hundred.

Such is Shanghai 41

— Qi Wo

S.M.P. is the abbreviation for [Shanghai Municipal Government]. Ah! Foreigners establish a municipal government in Shanghai, so what country does Shanghai belong to?

Rickshaw pullers call the British Concession permits [Big British Permits], and the Chinese territory permits [Small Permits]; people generally call Western food [Big Dishes], and Chinese food [Small Dishes]. Why are they so humble?

Foreign soldiers strut down the side of the road, and if a Chinese person walking more slowly blocks their path, they reach out and push them aside, then proudly walk past without even turning their heads. Ha! Foreign-capital companies and foreign firms stand in rows. Foreign managers lean back on sofas and smoke cigars with an air of superiority, while Chinese puppets run around all day long, busy scraping the fat off their compatriots.

Alas! Such is Shanghai!

Ke Xian Rice's Appetite is Strong

The situation of Ke Xian rice yesterday: Over 7,000 bags newly arrived, shipped by Ning Shao, Xin Ning, and Xin Jiang. With the increased appetite yesterday, sentiment has been upward, but the arrival of new Jiangxi rice has kept the market level. Japanese Troops Skirt Around and Invade Lingnan 48

Fierce Battles on All Fronts of Rehe Province Amidst Heavy Snow

The Japanese Army's Primary Targets Are to Seize Chifeng and Lingyuan

The Cui Brigade Repels Large Groups of Mongolian Bandits on the Kailu Front

Japanese Aircraft Continue to Bomb Chaoyang, Lingyuan, and Other Locations

(Beiping) Tang Yulin telegraphed from the 24th, reporting to Beiping that battles had broken out on the Lingyuan border. Lingnan and Kailu were extremely tense. The Japanese army was preparing to attack Chifeng from Kailu in the north and Lingyuan from Lingnan in the south. Currently, the Japanese army is using motor vehicles to transport troops along the road. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Sixty armored vehicles filled with Japanese soldiers departed from Jinzhou yesterday morning and advanced towards Lingnan last night. This morning, artillery fire was heard from Ling, initiating provocations. We are fully prepared and vow to strike fiercely. (25th Dispatch) (Beiping) With the Japanese army already commencing its attack on Kailu, the events in Rehe have taken a definitively formal shape in Tokyo. Their advance towards Kailu suggests their aim is Chifeng, located one hundred li northwest of Chengde. As for their advance towards the Chaoyang area, it appears their target is Lingyuan, less than one day's journey northwest of Shanhaiguan. Chifeng and Lingyuan are two essential passes for entering the central part of the province. If the Chinese army wishes to mount an effective resistance, it must spare no sacrifice in defending these two mountain passes. The defense of Lingyuan is especially solid. According to foreign military experts, the Chinese army there is determined and should be able to resist the Japanese army for at least several weeks, or even indefinitely. The Japanese army's advance on Kailu is progressing rapidly. However, volunteer troops guard the area between Tongliao and Kailu, so they must first fight the volunteer troops before encountering genuine resistance from the Chinese army. The Japanese army's actions in attacking Chaoyang are currently not considered noteworthy, so the Japanese army is now attempting a large-scale encirclement to the south to pressure Lingyuan. However, according to official reports, the Japanese army's attempts have made little progress. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

(Beiping) A report received from Tang Yulin today states that the Japanese army and [Manchu] troops are actively attacking Rehe, but to date, the Japanese army has not yet engaged with formal Chinese troops, having only encountered volunteer troops. These hardy volunteer troops, in the icy, snowy northern terrain, will inflict heavy blows on the Japanese army. The Japanese army encountered fierce resistance from the Chinese army when approaching Chaoyang Temple. Due to the solidity of the Chinese army's lines, the Japanese army's frontal assault has failed. Currently, Japanese troops are attempting to encircle to the south, with Lingyuan as their target. Japanese reinforcements are moving from Suizhong towards Rehe, also clearly aiming for Lingyuan. Operations are also underway near Kailu. The total number of Japanese troops is estimated to be at least 60,000, in addition to some [Manchu] troops participating in the operations. The Japanese air force is currently finding it difficult to operate due to adverse weather conditions, making reconnaissance and bombing difficult. Previous reports from Tokyo of mutinies by Chinese troops in Rehe have been strongly denied here. According to a European military expert recently returned from Rehe, the Chinese army's defense is extremely sound. If they can hold, the Japanese army will need to increase its forces to more than twice their current total to succeed in their attack. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

(Beiping) According to official reports, Japanese planes again carried out heavy bombing raids over Chaoyang, killing many civilians and destroying countless homes. Japanese planes are also conducting daily reconnaissance over the Chifeng area, but are afraid to fly low due to intense anti-aircraft fire. Official reports also state that after the Japanese army's frontal assault on Chaoyang failed, they have retreated and are reorganizing at Chaoyang Temple. Another column that has moved out from Suizhong is advancing towards Lingnan, aiming to threaten the rear of the Chinese army at Chaoyang. However, the Lingnan area is a continuous range of mountains, and the Japanese army's advance must pass through narrow mountain valleys. Machine guns are densely placed on the high ground of the four mountains, and the enemy army will be unable to overcome this great danger. According to news from Linyu, 4,000 [Manchu] soldiers have arrived from Suizhong to support the Japanese army. Reports of the fall of Kailu have not been verified. Official reports were still being sent from there last night, stating that Manchu and Mongolian troops had repeatedly attacked but were repelled. (25th Reuters Dispatch)

(Beiping) Kailu, 7:00 PM on the 24th: Heavy snow has fallen for days, and the temperature is two degrees below zero. However, the fighting between the two sides is extremely fierce today. This morning, a large number of Mongolian bandit cavalry, under the cover of Japanese artillery fire, set out from the Bilin Temple and launched three fierce attacks on our positions. Our Cui Brigade calmly responded, inflicting heavy casualties on the Mongolian cavalry, which ultimately failed to achieve their goal. In the afternoon, a large force of Japanese and traitorous allied troops attacked again, engaging in a stalemate in the Zhaoge Temple area for three hours before retreating without success. In this battle, our Cui Brigade captured three aircraft and more than a hundred Mongolian bandits, as well as numerous horses. (25th Dispatch)

The Dong Brigade Repels Enemy Troops at Beipiao

(Beiping) Tang Yulin telegraphed Beiping this afternoon, reporting that he received a telegram from Brigade Commander Dong on the morning of the 24th, stating that more than 3,000 Japanese troops, using armored vehicles as cover, attacked the Nanling Road positions. The Dong Regiment of our army ambushed within the trenches of Nanling to meet the enemy. The Japanese army launched several assaults, engaging in close combat with bayonets. Our army used hand grenades to bomb the enemy, whose corpses littered the ground. At 4:00 PM on the 23rd, the combat troops launched a full-scale counterattack from their defensive positions towards Beipiao. Reinforcements also arrived at the time, and the traitorous troops were ultimately defeated. The enemy and our side suffered heavy losses. The enemy at Koubeiyingzi are currently being pursued. Japanese planes have been flying to Chaoyang Sanbaoyingzi and our positions for days, carrying out bombing raids, etc. (24th Dispatch)

Japanese Planes Fly to Lingyuan and Drop Bombs

(Beiping) A telegram from Lingyuan states that Japanese planes have been flying to conduct reconnaissance and drop bombs for days. On the 22nd, two planes reconnoitered and dropped two bombs in the Shantou area. On the 23rd, four planes flew in formation over Lingyuan, dropping more than ten bombs. (25th Dispatch)

(Beiping) Lingyuan, 24th: Japanese planes have been flying in for days to drop heavy bombs, causing many innocent civilians to be injured. Civilian houses inside and outside the city have been severely damaged. However, our defensive positions have natural cover and cannot be destroyed by air power. (25th Dispatch)

The Enemy Headquarters is Established in Suizhong County

(Beiping) The enemy's headquarters for the attack on Chaoyang is located outside the South Gate of Suizhong County. As the Japanese Army Launches a Large-Scale Attack on Rehe, Our Representative Asks the League of Nations to Take Effective Action 57

The Advisory Committee is Officially Established 58

Continues to Handle the Sino-Japanese Dispute

The United States and Russia are Expected to Participate in Cooperation

(Geneva) During the continued meeting of the League of Nations General Assembly tonight, Chairman Hymans proposed a resolution and then invited Chinese representative Dr. Gu Weijun to speak, but asked him not to touch upon the remarks made by Japanese representative Matsuoka this morning. Therefore, Gu's speech was limited to the situation in Rehe, explaining the danger of the situation in Rehe and asking the General Assembly to authorize the committee to take necessary steps before adjournment so that the effective actions of member states and non-member states can be realized as soon as possible. Dr. Gu stated that the Chinese representatives are prepared to assist the committee's work in any possible way. The recent document sent by the Japanese delegation to the League of Nations has proven that Japan has absolutely no reason to indulge its ambitions in Rehe. Tang Yulin has never declared Rehe independent. Japan has raised doubts about China's sovereignty over its own territory, which directly denies the right of national existence and destroys the basic principles of international law. This document from Japan contains a warning. What right does Japan have to demand that China withdraw its troops guarding its territory? The so-called [Manchukuo] is not only a puppet, but also a mask for Japan's militarism. Judging from the conclusions of the Lytton Commission's investigation team and the League of Nations General Assembly report, the so-called Japan-[Manchu] agreement is actually a confession of guilt by Japan itself. We must devote all our efforts to resist aggression. The Japanese spokesperson claimed that it was unnecessary. Japan's claim that it does not want to attack Beiping and Tianjin is a way for Japan to announce the second object it wants to obtain. Yesterday's Japanese note was simply a declaration of war. Please also pay attention to the system of joint sanctions against aggressor countries when they are incorrigible, as recorded in the Covenant. Is there any doubt about Japan's illegal war of aggression? In this critical situation, only by taking swift action in accordance with the Covenant and implementing sanctions can the world know that the League of Nations values the League of Nations' justice and earnestly carries out its highest mission. What is this mission? It is international peace! After Gu completed his speech, Chairman Hymans asked if anyone else wished to speak. No one responded. The chairman then announced the end of the discussion. The chairman also said that if no one objected to the draft resolution he had proposed, it would be considered passed. There were no objections, and the resolution was declared passed. The General Assembly then adjourned. (24th Reuters Dispatch) (Geneva) It is still uncertain whether the Japanese delegation's posture in the meeting today was merely a demonstration or a prelude to genuinely severing relations with the League of Nations. Many feel that Japanese representative Matsuoka's second speech, in which he said that Japan has now reached the limit of its willingness to cooperate with the League of Nations regarding the Sino-Japanese dispute, was ambiguous in its meaning. However, it is expected that the Japanese government will soon reveal its position. There may not be immediate developments in Geneva, but it is only temporary. The newly formed 21-member committee will meet tomorrow to issue invitations to the United States and Russia. The United States is expected to accept, and Russia may also join. If so, the committee will not waste much time waiting for the representatives of the two countries to arrive. Mediation procedures have now been exhausted, so the League of Nations has no room for activity for the time being. However, once the US representative joins, the committee will be greatly encouraged, and the development of the situation in Rehe may also give the League of Nations reason to take a stronger stance. Chinese representative Dr. Gu mentioned the sanctions that the League of Nations could adopt in his speech this afternoon, so it is expected that China will request the application of Article 16 of the Covenant due to the invasion of Rehe. It is said that even if Japan withdraws from the League of Nations, it must fulfill all its international obligations under Article 1 of the Covenant. In other words, Japan will still be subject to various sanctions within the League of Nations' jurisdiction. It is generally hoped that Japan will not withdraw from the Disarmament Conference, otherwise international efforts to ensure peace through disarmament will suffer a fatal blow. Now that Germany and Italy have expressed their unyielding nature, and Japan has withdrawn from the League of Nations, and the war clouds in the Far East are becoming more and more diffused, the hope for a real achievement of the Disarmament Conference is almost non-existent. According to general opinion, the future of naval disarmament is not very optimistic. (24th Reuters Dispatch)

Japanese Newspaper Discusses the Reasons for the League of Nations' Anti-Japanese Stance 63

The Tokyo Hochi Shimbun published an article stating that since the Sino-Japanese issue arose, various countries have shown great jealousy towards Japan. The reason for this is not entirely due to the Sino-Japanese issue, but because the countries' own positions and interests have led to this. The underlying motives of various countries in deliberating the Sino-Japanese issue are analyzed below: (1) South American countries have no direct interest in the Far East and hope that the alliance will establish the authority to adjudicate belligerent countries, forcing them to accept the alliance's resolutions. This is something that South American countries must do for political reasons. (2) Ireland is a free state and has no relationship with either China or Japan. However, due to its anti-British hostility, the anti-Japanese actions of its representative, Mr. Lester, were very intense. (3) Representatives from small countries, such as Czechoslovak Foreign Minister Beneš, Swiss President Motta, Spanish Ambassador Madariaga, and Swedish representative Undén, want to promote the true power of the alliance in international politics and prevent attacks by neighboring great powers in the future. In other words, small countries are deeply afraid that problems similar to the Sino-Japanese one will occur again in Europe, so they are doing everything they can to promote the establishment of a precedent for fair action by the alliance. (4) France initially held a pro-Japanese attitude, but its sudden change of policy was due to two reasons: first, Germany was controlled by the Hitler faction; second, it was stimulated by the surrounding situation; and third, the international relations stipulated by the Treaty of Versailles should be firmly adhered to. If the alliance's regulations are not strengthened, it will suffer losses in the future. (5) Poland also has no great interest in the Far East and has no choice but to agree with the opinions of all parties. (6) Russia has always paid attention to Japan's Manchurian policy because the interests are very large. (7) Germany is currently in a chaotic domestic situation and does not want to take sides. (8) The United States believes that after Japan withdraws from the alliance, the United States can become closer to the alliance, and there is also news that the United States wants to join the alliance in 1935. Due to the above relationships, the anti-Japanese stance of various countries is actually within expectations.

Japan Continues to Transport Newly Enlisted Soldiers to the Northeast 70

Selecting Soldiers with the Strongest Cold Resistance

Prohibition on Speaking to Anyone Before Departure

A dispatch from the China United Press in Tokyo reports that although Minister of War Araki repeatedly states, "There is no need to increase troops in Manchuria," such statements are merely intended to conceal the actual evidence of his aggressive militarism. Since the opening of the Diet, in order to intensify the invasion of Jehol, troops have been continuously transported to the three northeastern provinces. In particular, newly enlisted soldiers are being secretly transported in large numbers, under the pretext of practical field training, to carry out aggressive deployment arrangements. The number of troop transports in January is listed below:

[January 17th] The Yamagata Garrison was ordered to begin organizing the formation of troops to be transported to Manchuria. As of recently, there are more than 3,000 people under the command of Major Aihara. [January 25th] The Kamiki unit and the Hirono Field Artillery unit, each with more than 300 people, departed twice from Hirosaki Station. [January 26th] The Hirono Field Artillery unit, the Miyake Garrison unit, and the Hayakawa Infantry unit also departed from Hirosaki Station in large numbers. [January 27th] The Tani Infantry unit departed from Aomori Station (twice). In addition, more than 800 newly enlisted soldiers of the Matsumoto Regiment, only one month after enlisting, were forcibly ordered to go to Manchuria for intense training. The team began shooting and sword fighting practice on January 22nd and 23rd, and departed from Matsumoto Station in full force on January 30th. It can be said that the entire Hirosaki 8th Division has been dispatched. The main force of this dispatch was selected from soldiers with the strongest cold resistance from the Tohoku region and Hokkaido areas of Japan. However, others, such as a portion of the Azabu 3rd Regiment and the Kofu Regiment, were moved to Utsunomiya, and then selected for departure from Utsunomiya, or directly dispatched from the Kansai and Kyushu areas. The above is only a portion of the investigation during railway transportation. The total number is impossible to investigate concretely, because the Japanese military department is keeping it absolutely secret. What is most noteworthy is that in order to prevent the soldiers being transported to Manchuria from being influenced by red ideas and anti-war propaganda, only two entrance tickets per family were allowed when departing, and only allowed to meet with newly enlisted soldiers. Any other person is absolutely prohibited from talking to the departing soldiers. The seriousness of the alert is evident.

Shantou Air Defense Association Promulgates

Regulations for Unsealing and Selling Enemy Goods

(Shantou) The Air Defense Association promulgated regulations for unsealing and selling enemy goods: (1) Goods stores pay 50% of the value as defense fee, (2) The value is determined by an appraisal committee jointly formed by the party department, the chamber of commerce, the air defense association, and the relevant trade associations, (3) Must be sold out within three months, and the tax is also divided into three installments and must not be delayed. Only the original enemy goods are allowed to be sold, (4) If new purchases are concealed, all the goods in the store will be confiscated and the shopkeeper and manager will be punished, (5) If any store has previously privately unsealed and sold them, the full value must be recovered as a fine, (6) The Air Defense Association makes certificates and gives them to merchants to sell with the certificates. This certificate is in triplicate, one for the Air Defense Association, one for the buyer, and one for the store, (7) If it is resold to operators, a resale certificate must be obtained before it can be sold, (8) Those who transport and sell to the interior must report the stub to the association and issue another transport and sales certificate to notify the National Salvation Associations in various places, (9) If the merchants still cannot sell out within three months, they will be concentrated by the chamber of commerce for auction, supervised by the National Salvation Association, the Air Defense Association, and the party department, (10) When the merchants have estimated the original goods, they will post a pledge at the door not to buy or sell enemy goods, (11) For all sealed enemy goods, if the store does not comply with these regulations, all the enemy goods in the store will be confiscated. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Shantou) The Shantou Su Guang Trade Association resolved that it is unwilling to unseal the goods to prevent new enemy goods from taking the opportunity to mix in and overwhelm the emerging domestic industries. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

(Shantou) Zheng Junying of the standing committee of the Air Defense Association said that the unsealing case has been resolved by various sectors and cannot be opposed in any way. (Special dispatch on the 24th)

Hitler Resolves to Unify All of Germany 84

Delivers a Speech to a Gathering of 30,000 People

Opposes the Restoration of the Bavarian State

A Reuters dispatch from Munich on the 24th reports that German Chancellor Hitler delivered a speech to a gathering of 30,000 people today in response to the threat from the Bavarian government authorities who proclaimed their intention to secede from the federal government. Hitler said that it is arrogant to want to turn Bavaria into a kind of Austria. If Bavaria makes such an attempt, it will inevitably destroy itself and fail. Hitler also said that his policy does not oppose anyone except the Socialist Party and the Communist Party. If any other political party wants to go to war, then he is prepared to defend the unity of Germany.

A Reuters dispatch from Berlin on the 24th reports that Interior Minister Dr. Frick said in a speech in Hamburg that any state that opposes the policies of the central government will be dealt with harshly if necessary.

A Reuters dispatch from Berlin on the 24th reports that Dr. Schäfer, chairman of the Bavarian People's Party, said in a speech in Wurzburg yesterday that if the central government sends administrative commissioners to Bavaria, they will be arrested as soon as they enter the country. He also said that if Berlin does not respect the German constitution and fairness, then Bavarians are free to choose the country they want to belong to. Dr. Schäfer ended by saying that when wild boars ran in the marshland where Berlin is located today, Bavaria was a civilized country.

A Reuters dispatch from Berlin on the 24th reports that Göring, the Prussian state interior administrator, in view of the increasing danger of the Communist Party, issued an order today to recruit auxiliary police to deal with the situation. This order is only valid in the state of Prussia. Applicants must be people who are inclined to the National Authority Party. They will wear plain clothes or uniforms and add special armbands. Some sources now believe that this move is to mobilize the National Socialist Party's stormtroopers to meet emergency needs and provide them with the rudiments of weaponry. Red newspapers all over Germany have been greatly trampled on, and the public is obviously dissatisfied. Today, Göring also issued an order to the Prussian state local officials, saying that the government will more strictly monitor newspapers that continue to despise the government from now on. Local officials must act more quickly and severely than before in the future.

Published at the City Government Reception for Newspaper Reporters

Sun Jimin's Declaration of Leaving the Communist Party 85

Reporting the Reasons for Leaving and the Process of Surrender

Stopping the Government's Anti-Japanese Course Again

Sun Jimin, secretary of the Jiangsu Provincial Committee of the Communist Youth League, member of the Presidium of the Central Executive Committee, and concurrently Minister of Organization, was indignant at the encroachment of foreign enemies and the critical situation of the country, deeply aware, and resolutely surrendered. At 10:00 this morning, the Information Office of the Municipal Government specially invited reporters from various newspapers to introduce them to Mr. Sun. First, Zhang Tingrong, director of the Information Office of the Municipal Government, and Wang Yonghua, director of the Special Affairs of the Public Security Bureau, introduced him. Then, Sun Jimin stood up and reported the reasons for leaving the Communist Party and the process of surrender. Mr. Sun joined the Communist Party in 1927, studied at the Moscow Chinese University, and returned to China in 1930. He served as the secretary of the Jiangsu Provincial Committee of the Communist Youth League, a member of the Presidium of the Central Executive Committee, and concurrently Minister of Organization. The following is a description of Sun's declaration of leaving the Communist Party:

Declaration of Leaving the Communist Party (1) History is replaying the raging tide of the Great Revolution of 1927, which was interfered with by imperialism and suffered great setbacks. However, if we believe that the failure of the Revolution of 1917 was solely due to the suppression of imperialism, then we have fallen into the trap of fatalism and have fundamentally abandoned the struggle to achieve a complete victory in the Chinese Revolution. The main reason for the failure of the Great Revolution was the error in the leadership of the revolution. However, the Chinese Communist Party's strategy of destroying the unified national line and dispersing the national revolutionary forces is responsible for this error. The current situation is even more serious than it was at that time. The three northeastern provinces have already fallen into the trampling and ravaging of Japanese imperialism, and Jehol and Tianjin are also under the threat of artillery fire from the Japanese warlords. However, although the 400 million people of China have been crying and wailing year after year, they have never been able to inflict a fatal blow on the successive attacks of Japanese imperialism. This is not due to the withering or decline of the Chinese nation, nor is it impossible to resist the blood of imperialism, but because of the division within China, because of the Chinese Communist Party's strategy of splitting the national revolutionary forces, destroying the national revolutionary front, because of the Chinese Communist Party launching strikes and student unrest, intensifying the execution of its bandit-style Soviet revolution, in order to disturb the rear, conspire to subvert the government, and obstruct the government's anti-Japanese line. This situation is no different from that in 1927. Although, the evolution of history is not without education for the 400 million masses of China. The Chinese Communist Party copied the Russian revolutionary experience, thinking that the Russian revolution took advantage of the opportunity of the war and implemented the strategy of [national defeat], [turning the imperialist war into a civil war] to seize political power in Russia, and attempted to [imitate it in China]. However, it is not known that China is a semi-colonial country, and striving for China's freedom and liberation and protecting the motherland is the demand of all Chinese people. The history of national liberation movements in the world proves the absurdity of the Communist Party's claims in the national liberation movement. The Russian revolution, although successfully by chance because of this, however, this wrong path of the Chinese Communist Party is enough to cause it to suffer a cruel defeat. Recently, the shrinking of the Soviet areas, the rapid retreat of urban work, and the Communist Party's separation from the peasant masses, the evolution of history is eliminating the Communist Party's base in China scene by scene.

(2) The honor and disgrace of the Chinese nation and the life and death of the people are completely entrusted to the success or failure of the anti-Japanese war, and whether China can concentrate its national strength to unanimously oppose foreign countries is a prerequisite for the victory of this war. Please see what the Chinese Communist Party has done, none of which is not betraying the interests of the nation. (1) At a time when the national crisis is imminent and Manchuria and North China have fallen under the artillery fire of Japanese imperialism, the Chinese Communist Party is taking advantage of the government and the people concentrating their forces to resist Japan and defend against insults, and then orders the general mobilization of the Red Army throughout the country to strive for the so-called first victory in one or several provinces. In the so-called Soviet area, it implements horizontal levies and violent exactions, and forcibly extracts able-bodied men, so that the people in the Soviet area are groaning and their cries are shaking the sky. Recently, it has taken advantage of the Jehol Incident, with the Red Army in Jiangxi and Fujian as the main force, and the Red Army in Sichuan, Shaanxi, Hubei, Henan, etc. as the response, to capture Fuzhou and Nanchang.

Dissatisfaction with military actions, so in the name of the commander-in-chief of the Red Army, he issued a declaration of a general declaration of war against Japan. In fact, this kind of ostrich policy is enough to expose its betrayal of the nation and its conspiracy to destroy the anti-Japanese war. Does the existence of the Red Army in the Chinese Soviet area have any revolutionary significance other than destroying the anti-Japanese war? Even members of the Chinese Communist Party cannot justify it. Even in terms of Marxism and Leninism, the success or failure of the revolution depends on the city as the main factor and the countryside as the guest. However, the Chinese Communist Party falsely exaggerates its bandit policy and then exaggerates, thinking that the leaders of the Chinese revolution are the Red Army and the Soviets who are hidden in the ancient temples of the mountains and forests. Isn't it a daydream? Judging from the facts, wherever the Red Army has set foot, nothing has been done, the land has been barren, the population has been sharply reduced, and the culture has been destroyed. In the past, it was thought that the evil signs in the Soviet area were caused by the Autumn Harvest Uprising line and the Li Lisan half-Trotsky line, but today the Communist Party leadership is everywhere touting the international line and decorating it with Leninism. Then who is to blame? Therefore, the unsuitability of communism to China's national conditions is an iron logic. Even if the Chinese Communist Party hits a wall for another fifteen years, it will not be able to argue. Does the existence of the Red Army in the Chinese Soviet area have any other significance other than destroying the national revolution and splitting the anti-Japanese war? (2) Use the decline of China's economy caused by the imperialist offensive to panic the production of workers and instigate workers to strike, causing chaos in the cities in order to fulfill its conspiracy to destroy production, making workers' lives more painful and increasing the number of unemployed workers. The Chinese Communist Party's strategy of manufacturing strikes and forcing workers to strike has actually reached the end of the road. All the experiences of strikes and struggles have proved that workers' spontaneous struggles can often be victorious, while the struggles led by the Communist Party often fail. This is not accidental, because the strikes led by the Chinese Communist Party are not to protect the interests of the workers, but to sacrifice the interests of the workers in order to create chaos in the rear and deepen the crisis in China's economy in order to weaken the Chinese nation's strength to resist Japan. The leaders of the Chinese Communist Party often blame the mistakes of the lower-level organizations for their inability to carry out strikes and struggles in China. However, facts speak louder than words. All major strikes and struggles have been discussed by the Standing Committee of the Central Committee, and even directly commanded by the Standing Committee. However, these events have suffered even greater failures. Even the much-anticipated yarn factory union, which caused a sensation in the party, was only a flash in the pan, and now it has completely disappeared. In the history of the Chinese Communist Party, there has never been a more serious fact of detachment from the workers than now. Perhaps the leaders of the Chinese Communist Party think that this is only a temporary accidental phenomenon, but anyone with a little insight can understand that in China, where national enthusiasm is soaring, it is impossible to take labor-capital disputes as the backbone of its activities, even if it succeeds by chance. (3) The Chinese Communist Party pays special attention to the peasant movement in the areas invaded by Japanese imperialism. Since the so-called Northern Conference denied the imbalance of the development of the Chinese revolution, it has stepped up the deployment of peasant guerrilla warfare in Manchuria, Shandong, Hebei, and other places, because peasant riots in those places can best obstruct the departure of the national army to fight against the Japanese army. The guerrilla war in Rizhao, Shandong, and the peasant riots in Gaoyang and Lixian, Hebei, were all launched from this perspective. As a result, they can only end up with cruel failures. The above points are only a dissection of the current strategy and line of the Chinese Communist Party in the large direction. However, the Communist Party's fate is not only manifested in its policy.

(3) The internal strife within the Chinese Communist Party is particularly fraught with dark secrets. In recent years, so-called opportunist lines have emerged one after another within the Communist Party, and there has been no relatively stable period. After the Li Lisan line, Chen Shaoyu, Qin Bangxian, etc., monopolized power, excluded dissidents, used private people to show their importance, and were insidious and arbitrary, so that everyone felt insecure, forming a divided state within the Communist Party. Recently, Communist Party members have been leaving and surrendering one after another, which is also the result of the Communist Party's erroneous leadership line. We believe that in the near future, due to the Communist Party's line hitting a wall and the awareness of lower-level personnel, the internal disintegration of the Communist Party will become even more uncontrollable. Our years of experience working in the Communist Party have made us finally realize the mistakes of the past and resolutely leave the Communist Party. We believe that there are still countless excellent young people in the Communist Party who have been misled by momentary impulses and have gone astray. They will use their own experiences to understand their mistakes and repent and stand together under the banner of the Three People's Principles and work hard for the liberation of the Chinese nation. Although we have declared our departure from the Communist Party organization, we are still willing to maintain private feelings for friends we have known in the Communist Party in the past. If there are those who sympathize with the country and the nation, or those who are still hesitant, and ask for advice, please send a letter to Shanghai Post Office Box 2150, and we will answer them one by one. Sun Jimin, February 1933 in Shanghai.

Shooting Accident Caused by Annamite Police Arrest in Xinqiao Street 86

One Killed, Three Injured

At 2:00 p.m. today, two women were riding in a rickshaw, heading north on Minguo Road and entering Xinqiao Street. When passing the Ningbo Hotel, they happened to encounter Annamite constable No. 427 who stepped forward to stop them, claiming that two people cannot ride in a rickshaw together. At the same time, he dug down the rickshaw's license. The woman got out of the car by herself. The rickshaw puller wanted the Annamite constable to return the license because it was dug out, but the constable firmly refused, and must bring the rickshaw puller and two women into the police station together. The two women said that they had something to do, and claimed that they were willing to pay a fine of five jiao to settle the matter, but the constable still refused and beat the rickshaw puller, which aroused the dissatisfaction of onlookers, who gathered to reason with and mediate with the constable. The constable fired a shot at the crowd with a rifle, and the crowd dispersed in all directions. When the Annamite constable fired the gun, Zhu Guting, the clerk of Renhe Grain Store at No. 61 Shoulu Lane, Xinqiao Street, was the first to be hit. The bullet penetrated his abdomen, and fresh blood gushed out, and the large intestine also flowed out of the abdomen with the blood, and he died on the spot. There was still a man behind him, and two women on the rickshaw were also hit by bullets, and their injuries were very serious. After the accident, all the detectives of the French Concession heard the news and rushed to the scene, and took the constable who caused the accident back to the police station, and sent the three injured people to the hospital. The body of the deceased Zhu Guting was sent to Tongren Fuyuantang to wait for the court to examine it.

Free Talk

A New Interpretation of "Rebellion" 93

— Tian Li

Since the Japanese occupation of our three northeastern provinces [September 18th Incident] last year and the League of Nations meetings, all dictionaries have had to be rewritten. For example, "aggression" should be interpreted as "self-defense," and "puppet" should be called "independent state." Old dictionaries of ancient history certainly cannot find such a brand new interpretation. The redefinition and completion of everything, such as "organization," "war," and "peace," must be credited to the efforts of the Japanese. This has not only refreshed the dictionary world but is also a monumental work of epoch-making significance. How great! Recently, we have seen a new interpretation of the word "rebellion."

According to a Reuters dispatch on the 20th, the Japanese cabinet, in a report to the special committee, declared that the League of Nations falsely accused our government of sheltering "rebels." This use of the word is truly novel and gratifying, and it is no less than a major discovery in the diplomatic world of the 20th century. I think that apart from the Japanese military and diplomatic circles who created this term, the more than 1.4 billion people in the world can only admire it!

The Japanese are acting out their oriental character very well. They are good at turning over history and seeking antiques. University professors are vigorously advocating that Manchuria and Mongolia are not Chinese territories. It is a pity that they have not deduced it to before the Ming and Qing dynasties, and they have not even mentioned that Korea is a descendant of Jizi. The military has even found the useless Puyi and used him as a cover. With this pitiful monkey, the show can be watched. The dogs who usually tuck their tails also began to wag, and then they pieced together a "puppet state," and then they talked about the so-called "royal way and benevolent government," and then there was the live drama of the so-called "punishing rebels." How terribly nauseating and interesting! This joke is no less than "looking for a donkey while riding one." Here, the Japanese creativity 丨丨 no, it is remaking 丨丨 is not inferior to imitation.

Speaking of "rebellion," the ancient saying is "great rebellion against the Way," which is similar to the meaning of today's "counter-revolution," or perhaps even worse. Hearing these two words, all people involuntarily solemnly and respectfully associate them with the words "extermination of the clan" and "slow slicing." Who is not afraid to say it? But now it comes unintentionally, which is truly excessive. The Japanese are truly good at sophistry. Fortunately, the Japanese use region to determine "obedience" and "rebellion," so only General Zhu Jiqing and Chairman Tang Yulin, who are fighting against the bandits on the front line, and the general Northeastern Volunteer Army are worthy of this crime. From a historical point of view, we were once slaves of the "Great Qing Dynasty." Now that the slaves have actually ascended the throne, the crime of rebellion does not need to be reviewed and is approved to be executed at the Meridian Gate. I think this day will always come, 丨丨 at least it will be proposed, as for whether the head will be cut off, it all depends on whether we rebel thoroughly!

Now I want to say that we have rebelled, we have rebelled. The "Great Qing" overthrew the dragon throne, rebelled against Japan, 丨丨 did not submit to the empire and surrender, but who did Japan rebel against? I want to ask all the 1.25 billion oppressed masses in this world.

New Method of Making Sugar from Scientific Maple Trees 94

— Nu

In the current time of national crisis, the voices of resisting foreign goods and promoting domestic goods are rising high into the clouds, but they are all verbal resistance. As for practical resistance, there are very few. Therefore, we do not need to talk about resistance, only about promotion methods. The reporter only seeks to discuss the item of white sugar in food products. The annual imports from foreign countries, if one checks the customs registers, the number should be surprising. Therefore, we cannot fail to pay attention to it and study the manufacturing methods to achieve practical resistance. Here is a list of the maple tree sugar making methods, and I hope that the people of the country will pay attention to it.

(1) Shape of maple tree: Maple tree is a deciduous tree with leaves shaped like palms. In March and April, it blooms with small red flowers. The fruit has two wings and uses wind power to spread the seeds. It is similar to maple trees and contains sugar, which is very suitable for sugar making.

(2) Taking: In late spring and early summer, the maple sap is most abundant, so at this time, cut an A-shape on the tree trunk and connect it with a bamboo tube. After about ten minutes, sap will flow out of the tube. Use a container to hold it below, but the best time to take the sap is in the morning. If the tree sap is exposed to sunlight and evaporated too late, it will form a crust and be difficult to flow down.

(3) Filtering impurities: Use white silk to make a bag shape, pour the obtained tree sap into the bag, and slowly squeeze it with force. The flowing sap can be put into a pot for cooking and refining.

(4) Cooking and refining: Pour the filtered sap into an iron pot, add fire to steam and cook, and stir with a stick at any time to prevent the sap at the bottom of the pot from burning. If it is burnt, it will taste bitter. After about two hours, the sap gradually thickens into a paste, then reduce the heat and add eggs and milk (about four eggs per fifty catties of thick sap), and five liang of milk.) After mixing evenly, if you see debris and bubbles floating up, use a copper wire mesh to filter them out. After twenty minutes, you can turn off the heat and remove the lid. At this time, the tree sap in the pot will solidify into a semi-fluid when it cools.

(5) Place in an enamel container about three feet five inches long, two feet wide, and three feet high. There are countless small holes at the bottom of the container. Lay a layer of cloth on the bottom, and pour the tree sap that is about to solidify in the pot into the enamel container. At this time, the honey contained in the tree sap will leak out from the small holes. Use a container to hold it, and what you get is pure white sugar.

News of Spring 95

— Wenbing

Spring has come, and the news brought by spring is a trembling of a beautiful painting in nature, and an entangled battle of ten thousand miles of flames among people.

People who are accustomed to living in cities do not feel the change of seasons very much. The oldest nation with a long history is most afraid of sinking into decline.

For example, Shanghai, with its dazzling scenery and towering buildings, has dozens of miles of land all artificialized, with layers of stone and layers of mud, and thick asphalt glued together. Grass and trees cannot take root, and the ground becomes a uniform color in all seasons. There is no fragrance of flowers in spring, no green shade in summer, no colorful red leaves in autumn, and no desolate desolation in winter. Rich young masters and ladies, and wealthy young women, immersed in such an environment, naturally only know that the weather is warm and change into light gauze, and the weather is cold and put on fur coats. Therefore, some people say that people in the city mostly only experience the change of temperature, which is indeed a fitting description.

Our national history is indeed long. From the Yellow Emperor to the present, it has been more than 4,000 years. If we trace back further to Pangu and the pre-historic period, we do not know how many ages there are. One vein has been turning back and forth in the feudal whirlpool. Throughout the dynasties, there have been many foreign races who have ruled. The common people only know that it is the succession of imperial luck and do not feel the sorrow of national decline. You say that the people of Egypt, India, and Goryeo are suffering now? Everyone really doesn't believe it, or they know it so they are startled and alert and invigorate themselves. Ah, the long history and the seniority are the roots of our nation's lack of a way out.

It is already early spring, and spring's smile is already baking in the countryside, but Shanghai is still no different from harsh winter. The city of Shanghai is indeed too big to bear

Page 22

The universal illumination of spring.

The nation has reached the line of peril, and the people of the country are still sleeping soundly. At the beginning of the September 18th Incident, it seemed that everyone was still a little angry. During the January 28th Incident, the people of the country once ran around and shouted in an atmosphere of emergency, but what about now? Although the hot war is erupting fiercely, the people of the country are just silent. Apart from some newspapers slightly drumming, what else can we hear?

Especially after the January 28th Incident, Shanghai was simply僵化. Has the flourishing national spirit of the past been extinguished by the gunfire of the Japanese in one fell swoop?

This terrible spring in the city, this terrible decline of the old nation!

If you want to return to the true origin, only the residents of the city can disperse to the countryside!

To transcend the nation, everyone must go to the front line! The news brought by spring is half good and half bad. The good is the beautiful scenery given by nature, which intoxicates our body and soul! The bad is the violent attack of the raging sun on Jehol, plundering. We need to rise up from intoxication, accept the gift of natural beauty, and go to shoot our enemies together.

We should not be too optimistic about the news brought by spring, nor should we only sigh. The era has arrived, and the nation needs our efforts.
